# Skyrim:Bards College

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Guild Hall: Bards College ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bards+College)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Bards_College "Lore:Bards College")) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[The Buying Game](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Buying_Game "Skyrim:The Buying Game")* *[Song of the Alchemists](/wiki/Skyrim:Song_of_the_Alchemists "Skyrim:Song of the Alchemists")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| SolitudeBardsCollege | |
| Location | |
| [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | |

Exterior of the College

The **Bards College** is a musical school in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). The Bards College is where any aspiring bard starts their career in [tale-telling or song](/wiki/Skyrim:Bardic_Performances "Skyrim:Bardic Performances"). It is located next door to [Proudspire Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proudspire_Manor "Skyrim:Proudspire Manor"), near the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace") inside the walls of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). The College, though large, contains few notable items. Many of the bards around [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") were trained at the College, and will recommend that the player visit the College. The primary reward for joining the college is actually three of its [miscellaneous quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Quests "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests"), which together grant +1 to every [skill](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") (18 points overall). The area contains only one zone, the [interior](#Bards_College).

## Joining the Bards College

Upon arriving at the Bards College, the player is able to seek admittance. It is traditional for new Bards to perform a service to the college before they can be admitted, but there is a problem. The headmaster [Viarmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Viarmo "Skyrim:Viarmo") will say that no new bards can be admitted except at the festival of the burning of King Olaf, which the bards have held annually, but this year the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair") wishes to cancel it as she feels it is in poor taste after the death of [her husband](/wiki/Skyrim:High_King_Torygg "Skyrim:High King Torygg").

Viarmo will ask you to help him reinstate the festival sending you on a [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames") to retrieve a document lost long ago, an epitaph written at the ancient time of King Olaf's passing, and which he believes will help change the Jarl's mind. The document can be found in [Dead Men's Respite](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Men%27s_Respite "Skyrim:Dead Men's Respite"). Once retrieved, return to Viarmo. You must help him fill in the gaps that are rampant in the document. Afterwards, the headmaster takes the player to the Jarl in order to try and reinstate the festival.

## Related Quests

Although there are a handful of quests associated with the Bards College, it does not have a true quest line. For example, there is no [knotwork](/wiki/Skyrim:Quests#Knotwork "Skyrim:Quests") specific to the Bards College, your game statistics do not have a separate category for tracking these quests, and there are no [achievements](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") for entering the college or finishing its quests. The following quests are instead categorized as a [side quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Side_Quests "Skyrim:Side Quests") and several [miscellaneous quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Quests "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests"):

### Side Quests

- **[Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames")**: Unveil the truth about a deceitful [King](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_One-Eye "Skyrim:Olaf One-Eye") and become a member of the Bards College.

### Miscellaneous Quests

- **[Investigate the Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Investigate_the_Bards_College "Skyrim:Investigate the Bards College")**: Investigate the Bards College.
- **[Finn's Lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Finn%27s_Lute "Skyrim:Finn's Lute")**: Return an invaluable [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Finn%27s_Lute_(item) "Skyrim:Finn's Lute (item)") to [Inge Six Fingers](/wiki/Skyrim:Inge_Six_Fingers "Skyrim:Inge Six Fingers").
- **[Pantea's Flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea%27s_Flute "Skyrim:Pantea's Flute")**: Find a missing [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea%27s_Flute_(item) "Skyrim:Pantea's Flute (item)") for [Pantea](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea_Ateia "Skyrim:Pantea Ateia").
- **[Rjorn's Drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Rjorn%27s_Drum "Skyrim:Rjorn's Drum")**: Retrieve a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Rjorn.27s_Drum "Skyrim:Quest Items") for [Giraud Gemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Giraud_Gemane "Skyrim:Giraud Gemane").

### Other Miscellaneous Quests

- **[Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery")**: Deliver an item to an associate. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Rare Gifts](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Gifts "Skyrim:Rare Gifts")**: Do a favor by finding a rare item. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Incomplete Quests

- **[Collecting the Edda](/wiki/Skyrim:Collecting_the_Edda "Skyrim:Collecting the Edda")**: Collect the parts of the Poetic Edda. ([unfinished](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfinished_Quests "Skyrim:Unfinished Quests"))

### Exterior

Three [barrels](/wiki/Skyrim:Barrel "Skyrim:Barrel") can be found on the corner of the courtyard across from the entrance. Two [Elven arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Arrow "Skyrim:Elven Arrow") and a [Potion of Plentiful Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Healing") can be found on the balcony.

### Ground Floor (Library and Trainer's Bedrooms)

The building itself has two entrances, the main entrance via the courtyard and the rear entrance that enters into the basement near the kitchen and student's quarters. There are a large number of books and musical instruments throughout the building and most of the crockery is of high quality.

Entry from the courtyard brings you into a reception area with a wooden bench against the northeast wall; in front of this is a low table holding a [platter](/wiki/Skyrim:Platter "Skyrim:Platter") with a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") on top and a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") of [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), while against the southwest wall is a set of shelves and a small unit with a [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") on a shelf and a [red mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") in a pot. To the southeast is a stairwell with stairs leading up to the top floor to the practice and lecture rooms and down to the basement to the kitchen and student's quarters. There is a red mountain flower on the end of the banister, in a pot, behind a large plant. On this floor the library is to the southwest and the teacher's bedrooms are to the northeast.

The library contains many common books on various bookcases, with tables and chairs arranged around the room. Some of the less common books found in the library include *[Feyfolken II](/wiki/Skyrim:Feyfolken_II "Skyrim:Feyfolken II")*, *[The Wild Elves](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wild_Elves "Skyrim:The Wild Elves")*, *[N'Gasta! Kvata! Kvakis!](/wiki/Skyrim:N%27Gasta!_Kvata!_Kvakis! "Skyrim:N'Gasta! Kvata! Kvakis!")*, *[On Stepping Lightly](/wiki/Skyrim:On_Stepping_Lightly "Skyrim:On Stepping Lightly")* and *[The Aetherium Wars](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Wars "Skyrim:The Aetherium Wars")*, which if you haven't read a copy previously will initiate a [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_to_the_Ages "Skyrim:Lost to the Ages") to investigate [Arkngthamz](/wiki/Skyrim:Arkngthamz "Skyrim:Arkngthamz"), a Dwemer ruin located in [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"). There is also a copy of *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")* which will initiate a misc quest to [find red eagle's sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn_(quest) "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn (quest)"). After starting [a quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Gifts "Skyrim:Rare Gifts") for [Lami](/wiki/Skyrim:Lami "Skyrim:Lami") to find a rare book, a copy of it, the [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Song of the Alchemists](/wiki/Skyrim:Song_of_the_Alchemists "Skyrim:Song of the Alchemists")* can be found on the counter in the library. On top of two of the bookcases against the southeast wall are a random [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing") [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") and a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka") while against the northeast wall is a small unit holding a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine").

To the northeast of the reception area is an internal wall with a small cupboard against it, following the corridor to the northwest, past two more cupboard, one on either side of the corridor, the first has a bunch of lavender on a shelf above it. The door at the end of the corridor leads into the bedroom belonging to [Viarmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Viarmo "Skyrim:Viarmo"), which contains a double four-poster bed coming out from the northwest wall with an end table on either side and a long unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing random items at the foot of the bed. Against the southwest wall is an open crate, behind the door containing a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") and a bunch of lavender, further to the right is a narrow wooden table with a platter holding two [baked potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") and a couple of pieces of cheese and a [plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate") of red and green apples. Against the northeast wall is a small wardrobe containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") and with a bunch of lavender on top. There is a washbasin to the right and a narrow wooden table beside that. In the eastern corner of the room is a dressing area with a cupboard against the northeast wall, with a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on top and a wall shelf holding an unlocked chest containing leveled items above it. Opposite this against the southwest wall are two tall wardrobe containing a mixture of fine clothes and clutter. On the corner of this wall, beside the door, is a large vase containing another bunch of lavender.

From the previous corridor there is another bedroom to the northeast belonging to [Pantea Ateia](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea_Ateia "Skyrim:Pantea Ateia") with a narrow wooden table outside against the northwest wall. This room contains a double bed coming out from the northwest wall with a small wardrobe on either side and a washbasin to the right in front of a basket containing a small coin purse. Against the southwest wall is a narrow wooden table with a bowl of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a plate holding a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and a bunch of lavender on top. Above this is a wall shelf holding a bunch of [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") and a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flower. Against the northeast wall is a narrow wooden table and a bookcase containing eight common books and a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute") with another book on the floor in front of it, while against the southeast wall is a wooden table with a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") and [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") on top, with a tall vase and wooden bench to the right of it.

The next bedroom along to the southeast belongs to [Inge Six Fingers](/wiki/Skyrim:Inge_Six_Fingers "Skyrim:Inge Six Fingers"). It contains a large single bed coming out from the northeast wall with an end table to the right. Against the southeast wall are two wall shelves holding a [potion of plentiful healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Healing") and a bunch of lavender. To the right of these is a narrow wooden table, while against the southwest wall is a wooden bench and corner shelf that holds a [potion of resist fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire"). Against the northwest wall are two pairs of bookcases separated by two more coming out from the wall. There bookcases hold a total of thirty-nine common books, including a copy of *[Walking the World, Vol XI](/wiki/Skyrim:Walking_the_World,_Vol_XI "Skyrim:Walking the World, Vol XI")*, which will update your map if you haven't discovered all of the places mentioned in and around [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). There are also two less common books, *[Charwich-Koniinge Letters, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Charwich-Koniinge_Letters,_v1 "Skyrim:Charwich-Koniinge Letters, v1")* and *[Invocation of Azura](/wiki/Skyrim:Invocation_of_Azura "Skyrim:Invocation of Azura")*, a [potion of extreme magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extreme_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extreme Magicka"), a [potion of extreme stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extreme_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Extreme Stamina") and a [solution of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Strength "Skyrim:Solution of Strength"). There is a low table and chair on the northern corner of the room with a single common book on top.

The last bedroom on this floor belongs to [Giraud Gemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Giraud_Gemane "Skyrim:Giraud Gemane") and is next door to the southeast of Inge Six Fingers' bedroom. It contains a single bed coming out diagonally from the southern corner with an end table to the right and an open crate at the foot of the bed. Against the southeast wall is a small wardrobe containing fine clothes and with a [potion of lasting potency](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Lasting_Potency "Skyrim:Potion of Lasting Potency"), a common book and a bunch of tundra cotton on top. Against the northeast wall is a wooden bench, while against the northwest wall are two wall shelves, both with a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute"), above a narrow wooden table. To the right are two sets of shelves holding a collection of flutes, drums, a lute and three common books. In front of these is a low table and chair with a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") and a bunch of lavender on top of the table and another drum on the floor in the northern corner. Outside Giraud's bedroom is a low table and chair with a bunch of lavender and a [potion of plentiful stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Stamina") on top of the table.

### Top Floor (Lecture/Practice Rooms)

At the top of the stairs there is a small cupboard on the left with a red mountain flower in a pot on top. Opposite the stairs in a small balcony that overlooks the reception area with a large planter holding two deathbell plants and an open crate containing ten common books. There is a second cupboard next to a wooden bench at the rear of the balcony, over the stairs. The corridor leads to rooms at the northeast and southwest ends of the building.

To the northeast there is a cupboard against the southeast wall with an open crate containing three more common books, opposite a small storeroom, which contains a small cupboard against the northwest wall and two sets of shelves against the northeast wall. These hold two [quicksilver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ingot "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ingot"), while opposite against the southwest wall are a stack of crates and a couple of rugs. The main lecture and practice room has a lectern on a raised dais at the northeastern end of the room over looking three wooden benches facing it. In the northern corner of the room is a planter containing a [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") plant, with a potion of health hidden among the leaves. Against the southwest wall are two wall shelves holding three common books, while against the northeast wall are two more wooden benches, with two more against the southeast wall separated by two pairs of bookcases back-to-back coming out from the middle of the southeast wall holding a total of thirty common books, including *[An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:An_Explorer%27s_Guide_to_Skyrim "Skyrim:An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim")* which adds map markers for [The Guardian Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Guardian_Stones "Skyrim:The Guardian Stones"), [The Lover Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lover_Stone "Skyrim:The Lover Stone"), [The Ritual Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ritual_Stone "Skyrim:The Ritual Stone") and [The Shadow Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Shadow_Stone "Skyrim:The Shadow Stone"). Some of the less common books on these shelves include a copy of *[The Pig Children](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pig_Children "Skyrim:The Pig Children")*, *[The Seed](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Seed "Skyrim:The Seed")*, *[Feyfolken I](/wiki/Skyrim:Feyfolken_I "Skyrim:Feyfolken I")*, a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill book *[The Buying Game](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Buying_Game "Skyrim:The Buying Game")* and a copy of *[Lost Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends")* which, if you haven't already initiated the [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Forbidden_Legend "Skyrim:Forbidden Legend") will add a map marker and direct you to [Folgunthur](/wiki/Skyrim:Folgunthur "Skyrim:Folgunthur"). There is also a low table in the eastern corner of the room with three common books on top. Against the southwest wall is a set of shelves holding a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health").

To the southwest in the corridor there are two small cupboards against the southeast wall, opposite two narrow wooden tables with three common books, a [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") and a bowl containing a sprig of snowberries on top. The main lecture and practice room at the end of the corridor has a lectern on a raised dais facing three wooden benches that have several drums and flute on them, to the southeast. There is a planter containing a deathbell plant in the northern corner, next to a narrow wooden table which has a sprig of snowberries on top against the northeast wall. At the rear of the room there is a set of shelves coming out from the southeast wall holding a couple of drums, a flute and a lute, with a planter containing two deathbell plants to the left and a wooden bench to the right. In the eastern corner there is a basket containing a potion of minor stamina, with a small cupboard to the left, against the northeast wall with a lute on top. Opposite this is a wooden bench against the southwest wall and a low table in front, with a bunch of tundra cotton, a sprig of snowberries and a flute on top.

### Basement (Kitchen and Student's Quarters)

Descending the stairs leads to an open area with two clusters of seating arranged around low tables and two small cupboards, one against the northeast wall and the other against the southwest wall. To the southwest is a large opening into the kitchen where [Bendt](/wiki/Skyrim:Bendt "Skyrim:Bendt") spends his days. It contains four long wooden tables, one against the against the southeast wall has a baked potato and two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") on top. One against the northwest wall has a bottle of alto wine and two more salmon steaks on top and a rack hanging above from the wall holding a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid, two bunches of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). The third is in the middle of the room between the other two and has a baked potato, two salmon steaks, two loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") and a platter holding another two baked potatoes, a sweet roll and two pieces of goat cheese. These three all have benches beside them.

The fourth table appears to be used for preparing [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") and is in front of the oven on the southwest wall. There is another baked potato and an empty pot in the oven, while on the table there are a [carrot](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), a [leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), three [tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"), two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), two bulbs of garlic, three fillets of [salmon meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Meat "Skyrim:Salmon Meat"), a sheaf of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") and a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"). In the eastern corner is a large round table and chair with a plate of bread and cheese on the table. Against the northwest wall is a small unit holding a bottle of alto wine, two bottles of [Honningbrew mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead") and a bottle of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead"), while in the southern corner are two sets of shelves holding four red apples, a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), a salmon steak, a fillet of salmon meat, a [slaughterfish egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg"), a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), five garlic bulbs, a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), two loaves of bread, a potato and several pieces of cheese. To the right of the oven is a rack hanging from the southwest wall with two cooked [horse haunches](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Haunch "Skyrim:Horse Haunch") and a raw haunch of [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison") above a wood pile and block with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") leaning against it.

To the right of these is a doorway to Bendt's L-shaped bedroom which contains a tall wardrobe against the southwest wall, with a dresser to the right that has a plate of bread and cheese on top. There is a single bed in the northern corner with a small low table beside it which has a copy of *[Uncommon Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:Uncommon_Taste "Skyrim:Uncommon Taste")* on top and against the southeast wall is a set of shelves holding a bottle of alto wine, a [chef's tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Chef%27s_Tunic "Skyrim:Chef's Tunic") and [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Chef%27s_Hat "Skyrim:Chef's Hat"), and a woodcutter's axe.

To the northeast is an area with several food sacks on the floor, while around the corner to the southeast there is a stack of crates and a small cupboard flanking the rear entrance. To the northwest is the student's quarters with a row of four single beds all coming out from the southwest wall, with a small table beside each of them and partitions separating each of them. The small tables have either a common book or small item of food on each. Against the northeast wall there are two tall wardrobes containing fine clothes, with a dresser at either end containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes").

## Notes

- For a complete list of the various Bard performances, see [this page](/wiki/Skyrim:Bardic_Performances "Skyrim:Bardic Performances").
- Even after being admitted into the college, the beds are not open for you to rest in, neither will you ever rise in ranks or take any active part in College business.
- Other than most barrels and sacks, all containers in the Bards College are [non-respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") and safe to store items in.

## Bugs

- For the three quests involving the retrieval of instruments, the script for removal of the quest items from one's inventory at the completion of the quest is bugged. As such, these items will permanently be in your inventory (they're flagged as Quest items). Owners of the PC version of Skyrim can use console commands to remove these items from their inventory.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
- Sometimes the objective "Investigate the Bards College" cannot be completed. Starting this quest after you have already joined the Bards College will make this quest incompletable, permanently leaving this task in your quest journal. The quest indicator points at the quest target but no dialogue options are present. You can clear the "Investigate the Bards College" quest by typing `SetObjectiveCompleted MS05Start 10 1` into the console.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- All class sessions can be started even if none of the students are present. The instructional lines from each teacher have a tendency to play from wherever they happen to be in the building.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, fixes this bug.
- If your first visit to the Bards College doesn't take place until after King Olaf's Verse has been recovered, the pointer quest to investigate the College may fail to terminate.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- After completing Battle for Solitude, the Imperial banners don't change for the Stormcloak ones. **?**

The barkeep tending his bar at Cragslane Cavern

The **Barkeep** is a hostile [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") found in [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern") serving drinks to the [gamblers](/wiki/Skyrim:Gambler "Skyrim:Gambler"). He wears [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0005b6a1 "Skyrim:Clothes") and [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes#0005b6a0 "Skyrim:Shoes") and is equipped with a leveled [one-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:One-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:One-Handed Weapons") (up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") quality). He carries a considerable amount of leveled gold, ranging from 25 to 125 gold, and the [Craglane chest key](/wiki/Skyrim:Craglane_Chest_Key "Skyrim:Craglane Chest Key") which opens the chest behind his bar.

## Related Quests

- **[Supply and Demand](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand")**: Clear [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern") for the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

# Skyrim:Barknar (Dawnguard)

## Overview

This article is about the refugee added by Dawnguard. For the ranger on the Throat of the World, see [Barknar](/wiki/Skyrim:Barknar "Skyrim:Barknar").

| Barknar (RefID: [xx](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID "Skyrim:Form ID")0198B5) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Added by | [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") | | |
| Location | [Dayspring Canyon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dayspring_Canyon "Skyrim:Dayspring Canyon") | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Dremora Class](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_(class) "Skyrim:Dremora (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | [xx](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID "Skyrim:Form ID")0198B5 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | [xx](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID "Skyrim:Form ID")0198B4 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 50 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 50 | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| Voice Type | [MaleNord](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleNord "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleNord") | | |

.jpg)

Barknar

**Barknar** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") camped out in [Dayspring Canyon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dayspring_Canyon "Skyrim:Dayspring Canyon"). He came to [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard") with his wife [Alvide](/wiki/Skyrim:Alvide "Skyrim:Alvide") for protection from the [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") but the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)") won't let him in.

He will show up in Dayspring Canyon during the quest [Beyond Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Beyond_Death "Skyrim:Beyond Death") and will do very little but wander around, at times chopping some firewood or using the [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"). He never sleeps. He wears [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#000261c0 "Skyrim:Clothes") with a [cowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Cowl#00017696 "Skyrim:Cowl") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000261bd "Skyrim:Boots").

## Dialogue

He will explain his situation, saying things like:

:   *"I've no love for living out of a tent, but I'll take that over being ripped apart."*
:   *"Why can't they just let us in? We won't get in the way!"*
:   *"It looks like this is as close as we're going to get being safe from the vampires."*
:   *"I hope Alvide doesn't think less of me, but I can't protect her on my own. We're safer here."*

## Notes

- Barknar does not have a unique facial model, he instead uses the default male Nord face. He shares this quirk with numerous other NPCs, including [Erikur](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur "Skyrim:Erikur"), [Sond](/wiki/Skyrim:Sond_(bandit) "Skyrim:Sond (bandit)"), [Lynoit](/wiki/Skyrim:Lynoit "Skyrim:Lynoit"), [Briehl](/wiki/Skyrim:Briehl "Skyrim:Briehl"), and many other generic NPCs.
- Strangely, Barknar lacks any kind of schedule. He will simply idle where he was put.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.2.3, addresses this issue. He has been given a default sandbox package.

# Skyrim:Barknar

## Overview

This article is about the ranger on the Throat of the World. For the refugee added by Dawnguard, see [Barknar (Dawnguard)](/wiki/Skyrim:Barknar_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Barknar (Dawnguard)").

| Barknar (RefID: 000BC07A) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home Town | [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") | | |
| Location | The 7,000 steps | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Ranger](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranger_(class) "Skyrim:Ranger (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000BC07A | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000BC079 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 50 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 50 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| Voice Type | [MaleNord](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleNord "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleNord") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [TownIvarsteadFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownIvarsteadFaction "Skyrim:TownIvarsteadFaction") | | |

Barknar

**Barknar** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [ranger](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranger_(class) "Skyrim:Ranger (class)") from [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") who often walks the path towards [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar").

He can be found praying in front of the second etched tablet you encounter as you climb the 7000 steps. Once found, he will start heading down the mountain, and go to the [Vilemyr Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilemyr_Inn "Skyrim:Vilemyr Inn") in Ivarstead where he will eat, relax, or sleep at random times. At other times, he may decide to take yet another trip up the mountain for another silent prayer.

He wears [hide armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor"), [gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Gloves#000261c1 "Skyrim:Gloves"), and a pair of randomly selected [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") (4 variants). He also has a 50% chance of wearing a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat "Skyrim:Hat") (3 variants). He carries a leveled [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") with twelve [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrow "Skyrim:Arrow") of the best possible quality. He also carries a spare set of gloves, a [torch](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch"), a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), and a small amount of gold. Barknar also carries 60 [fire arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Arrow "Skyrim:Fire Arrow") with the [Arcane Archer Pack](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Archer_Pack "Skyrim:Arcane Archer Pack") installed.

## Related Quests

- **[The Way of the Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Way_of_the_Voice "Skyrim:The Way of the Voice")**: Meet the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards").

## Quest-Related Events

When he sees you he will provide a bit of advice:

:   *"Keep an eye out for wolves if you're headed up the path to High Hrothgar."*

When asked if he heard the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards") summon the Dovahkiin, he will say:

:   *"I did. Strange days when the monks will do that. I wonder what it means."*

:   **What are you doing?**
:   *"I like to spend time up here. Walk the Steps, meditate on the emblems. Doesn't hurt when I bag some game along the way."*

:   **Do you visit the Greybeards?**
:   *"They're not the sort to take visitors, but I never go that high up the path anyway. Some folk who make the trip leave them food or other essentials, but not to make conversation."*

If you meet him later at Vilemyr Inn, you can ask him again what he is doing and he will respond:

:   *"Enjoying the hospitalities of the inn. Suggest you do the same."*

Lastly, if you meet him on his way up the mountain and ask what he is doing he will explain:

:   *"I'm walking the 7,000 Steps to honor the Greybeards and reflect on my own life. It's a tradition among the Nords of Skyrim."*

# Skyrim:Barracks

## Overview

Dawnstar Barracks

This page lists all the **guard barracks** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"). Each [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds"), with the exception of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)"), has its own barracks.

:   **[Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch")** — A hold in eastern Skyrim, with its capital in Windhelm.

    :    **[Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings")** — A large castle at the far end of the Valunstrad district in Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Palace+of+the+Kings)
:   **[Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold")** — A hold in southern Skyrim, with its capital in Falkreath.

    :   **[Falkreath Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Barracks "Skyrim:Falkreath Barracks")** — The living quarters for the Falkreath guards and also contains Falkreath Hold's jail. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Falkreath+Barracks)
:   **[Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar")** — A relatively small hold in northwest Skyrim, containing the provincial capital Solitude.

    :   **[Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour")** — A large fortress in Solitude which acts as the headquarters of the Imperial Legion and residence of the Emperor in Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Castle+Dour)
:   **[Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch")** — A hold in northern Skyrim, with its capital in Morthal.

    :   **[Guardhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Guardhouse "Skyrim:Guardhouse")** — The Hjaalmarch barracks on the south side of Morthal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Guardhouse)
:   **[Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A large island in the Sea of Ghosts northeast of Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Solstheim)

    :   **[The Bulwark](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bulwark "Skyrim:The Bulwark")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — An imposing stone wall created to protect Raven Rock from ash storms, with the city's garrison and jail both built directly into the wall. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=The+Bulwark)
:   **[The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale")** — A hold in northern Skyrim, with its capital in Dawnstar.

    :   **[Dawnstar Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Barracks "Skyrim:Dawnstar Barracks")** — The living quarters for the Dawnstar guards. It also houses Dawnstar's jail. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dawnstar+Barracks)
:   **[The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach")** — A hold in western Skyrim, with Markarth as its capital.

    :   **[Guard Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Tower "Skyrim:Guard Tower")** — A Dwemer tower in the center of Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Guard+Tower)
:   **[The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift")** — A hold in southeast Skyrim, with its capital in Riften.

    :    **[Mistveil Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistveil_Keep "Skyrim:Mistveil Keep")** — A castle located at the southern end of Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mistveil+Keep)
:   **[Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold")** — A hold in central Skyrim, with its capital in Whiterun.

    :   **[Guard Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Barracks "Skyrim:Guard Barracks")** — A building in Whiterun where guards live when not on duty. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Guard+Barracks)
    :   **[Guard Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Barracks_(Gate) "Skyrim:Guard Barracks (Gate)")** — A building near the main gate in Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Guard+Barracks)

# Skyrim:Bashnag

## Overview

| Bashnag (RefID: 0002B99D) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum") | | |
| Race | [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") | Gender | Male |
| Level | Radiant (1-46) | Class | [Conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer_(class) "Skyrim:Conjurer (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0002B99D | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000A33EA |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 50-575 | | |
| [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 100-500 | | |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 25-50 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration")**, **[Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration")**, [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration"), [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") | | |
| Class Details | [CombatMageConjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer "Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | Any Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Very Aggressive |
| Respawns | Yes | | |

Bashnag at an arcane enchanter

**Bashnag**, an [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer "Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer"), is the leader of the [spellsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellsword_(NPC) "Skyrim:Spellsword (NPC)") coven residing in [Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum"). He cast [Selveni Nethri](/wiki/Skyrim:Selveni_Nethri "Skyrim:Selveni Nethri") out of his circle of mages, cursed and chased her into a [spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") web, giving you the opportunity to save her as part of a [miscellaneous quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Savior_of_Selveni_Nethri "Skyrim:The Savior of Selveni Nethri").

He spends most, if not all, of his time at the [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") in the back of the dungeon. He always wears [ancient Nord armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Armor "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Armor"), but the rest of his equipment is leveled. His boots can be [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"), [steel cuffed](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Cuffed_Boots "Skyrim:Steel Cuffed Boots") from level 6, and [steel plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Boots "Skyrim:Steel Plate Boots") from level 18 onward. His gauntlets will always be enchanted with either [Fortify Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Apparel#Fortify_Alchemy "Skyrim:Generic Magic Apparel"), [Fortify Marksman](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Apparel#Fortify_Marksman "Skyrim:Generic Magic Apparel"), [Fortify One-Handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Apparel#Fortify_One-Handed "Skyrim:Generic Magic Apparel"), [Fortify Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Apparel#Fortify_Smithing "Skyrim:Generic Magic Apparel"), or [Fortify Two-Handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Apparel#Fortify_Two-Handed "Skyrim:Generic Magic Apparel"); and they can be [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets"), [steel Nordic](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Nordic_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Steel Nordic Gauntlets") from level 7, [Dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Dwarven Gauntlets") from level 13, [steel plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Steel Plate Gauntlets") from level 19, [Orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Orcish Gauntlets") from level 26, [ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Ebony Gauntlets") from level 33, [dragonplate](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonplate_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Dragonplate Gauntlets") from level 41, and finally [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Daedric Gauntlets") from level 49 onward. He also wears two pieces of unenchanted leveled jewelry, specifically a [ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring "Skyrim:Ring") and an [amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet "Skyrim:Amulet"). He wields a leveled [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), which can be [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Steel Mace"), [Orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Mace "Skyrim:Orcish Mace") from level 9, [Dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Mace "Skyrim:Dwarven Mace") from level 15, and [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Mace "Skyrim:Elven Mace") from level 22 onward. He also carries a leveled [staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Staves "Skyrim:Staves"), three random [gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems"), and some gold.

His spells are taken from the standard [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") spell lists. Technically speaking, he is an unnamed necromancer that will respawn, but has been given the name Bashnag through the related quest. In addition to a name, he's also been given a copy of the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Art of War Magic](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Art_of_War_Magic "Skyrim:The Art of War Magic")*, and the [Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing"), [Fast Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fast_Healing "Skyrim:Fast Healing"), and [Conjure Frost Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Frost_Atronach "Skyrim:Conjure Frost Atronach") spells. This simply means that when he respawns, he'll have a generic necromancer name, without the book and extra spells.

## Related Quests

- **[The Savior of Selveni Nethri](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Savior_of_Selveni_Nethri "Skyrim:The Savior of Selveni Nethri")**: Help a necromancer escape from [Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum").

## Notes

- With [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") installed, his equipment can also consist of [Nordic material](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic "Skyrim:Nordic").
- One internal reference names him "**Hacklecomb**".
- Bashnag almost never leaves the room he is found in under normal circumstances. This applies even to normal combat; if you are having trouble with him, run back the way you came and he very likely won't follow.

## Bugs

- He can be named generically as a necromancer instead of Bashnag when he is the target boss of a radiant quest.

# Skyrim:Bassianus Axius

## Overview

| Bassianus Axius (RefID: 00019E08) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home City | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") (After his quest) | | |
| Home Town | [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") | | |
| House | [Klimmek's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Klimmek%27s_House "Skyrim:Klimmek's House") | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 6 | Class | [Citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00019E08 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000136C1 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 91 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 67 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 67 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing"), [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| Voice Type | [MaleCondescending](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleCondescending "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleCondescending") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionRift](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionRift "Skyrim:CrimeFactionRift"); [IvarsteadKlimmekHouseFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:IvarsteadKlimmekHouseFaction "Skyrim:IvarsteadKlimmekHouseFaction"); [TownIvarsteadFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownIvarsteadFaction "Skyrim:TownIvarsteadFaction") | | |

Bassianus at the Vilemyr Inn

**Bassianus Axius** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") and a resident of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") where he works as a fisherman. A lover of [Fastred](/wiki/Skyrim:Fastred "Skyrim:Fastred"), Bassianus' desire is for both of them to leave for [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") against the wishes of Fastred's father, [Jofthor](/wiki/Skyrim:Jofthor "Skyrim:Jofthor"). Fastred herself is undecided on the matter and still has feelings for Bassianus' colleague and housemate, [Klimmek](/wiki/Skyrim:Klimmek "Skyrim:Klimmek"). During the quest [The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love") you will have to sort out the love triangle on behalf of [Mara](/wiki/Lore:Mara "Lore:Mara") and ensure things turn out the best for Fastred.

Ironically, Bassianus lives in the same [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Klimmek%27s_House "Skyrim:Klimmek's House") as his rival Klimmek, where he sleeps every night between 10pm and 4am. He starts the day with a one-hour breakfast with Klimmek then heads over to [Vilemyr Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilemyr_Inn "Skyrim:Vilemyr Inn") where he spends the entire day with the other regulars, sitting, conversing, or drinking. At 1pm and 6pm he pauses for one-hour meals. When triggering state 90 "Find Fenrig" of the related quest, he will move to Riften, though the choices you make in completing his portion of the quest will determine whether or not Fastred accompanies him. He was supposed to check in at [Haelga's Bunkhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga%27s_Bunkhouse "Skyrim:Haelga's Bunkhouse") and sleep there every night between 8pm and 4am, but doesn't due to a [bug](#Bugs). Instead, he will wander around Riften 24 hours a day.

He wears a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0001be1b "Skyrim:Boots"). He is equipped with a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") which can be up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") quality, and carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Klimmek%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Klimmek's House") to Klimmek's house, as well as a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love")**: Help the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") spread the cause of love throughout Skyrim.

## Dialogue

Bassianus and Klimmek arguing

Bassianus is not overly welcoming, and will greet you with:

:   *"You don't look like a pilgrim. Why bother visiting Ivarstead?"*
:   *"Hmm? What do you want?"*

Like the other Ivarstead citizens, he will tell you a bit about [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar"):

:   **Anything you can tell me about High Hrothgar?**
:   *"Klimmek brings food supplies up to them once every few weeks when the weather permits it. Other than that, they seem like a quiet lot. Don't really know too much about them."*

He will finish conversation with:

:   *"Hmph. What a boring conversation."*

### Conversations

The problems with Fastred have seemingly taken its toll on the relationship between the two fishermen. When they meet inside the house, they can be heard arguing:

**Bassianus**: *"If you have a moment, I've come up with a few ideas I wanted to share."*
**Klimmek**: *"I'm becoming sick to death of your ideas. Not one of them has paid off since you moved in."*
**Bassianus**: *"Look, I'm merely suggesting a few things that could expand our business."*
**Klimmek**: *"'Our' business? As I remember things, it was you that showed up at my doorstep looking for a job and a place to live. Try and remember that."*

**Klimmek**: *"We're behind again. I need you to catch another two bushels by week's end if I'm to make another delivery."*
**Bassianus**: *"Blood from a stone, Klimmek. I've been out there every morning. They just aren't biting."*
**Klimmek**: *"Come on, everyone in town knows that you spend more time with Fastred than fishing in the river."*
**Bassianus**: *"That's none of your business and I appreciate if you wouldn't mention it again."*

Bassianus' crush on Fastred is known all over town, and even local innkeeper [Wilhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Wilhelm "Skyrim:Wilhelm") will ask him about it:

**Wilhelm**: *"Have you spoken to Fastred yet?"*
**Bassianus**: *"No. I'll tell you, Wilhelm, if I could sweep her away from here tomorrow I'd do it, but Klimmek still has so much to learn."*
**Wilhelm**: *"Klimmek is doing just fine. You should follow your heart."*
**Bassianus**: *"Perhaps one day, but not today."*

### The Book of Love

If you choose to confront Bassianus at Boti's request:

:   **Boti said to talk to you about Fastred.**
:   *"Oh, my love. How I long to take her away from all of this. Why did Boti send you to me?"*

:   :   **I'm not sure. I hope things work out for you.**
    :   *"As do I. It's a puzzling situation."*

:   :   **She said that you should elope.**
    :   *"I always had a feeling she liked me. More than that brute Jofthor, at least. Jofthor... what about him? He'll come after us and... it will be unpleasant."*

        :   **Boti said she'd handle Jofthor.**
        :   *"She would? If she's willing to deal with him, then everything would be all right. I'll... I'll go speak to Fastred. Post-haste!"*

He will then run off to see Fastred, and this conversation will play:

*"Bassianus, sweetie, what is it?"*

**Bassianus**: *"Fastred, we must speak."*
**Fastred**: *"Bassianus, sweetie, what is it?"*
**Bassianus**: *"We must leave. Your father will never approve of us, and I grow weary of this place."*
**Fastred**: *"Where will we go?"*
**Bassianus**: *"To Riften, my pet. How you'll adore the city."*
**Fastred**: *"Oh, and to be with you!"*
**Bassianus**: *"I'll make the preparations immediately!"*

## Notes

- Bassianus (and Fastred, if you did not side with Klimmek) will teleport to Riften at [stage 90](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love#Quest_Stages "Skyrim:The Book of Love") (when you are told to find [Fenrig](/wiki/Skyrim:Fenrig "Skyrim:Fenrig")) of the related quest to ensure that you are nowhere near Ivarstead to witness the nonexistent journey.
- Curiously, Bassianus has an overtly Imperial name, but is considered a Nord in-game.

## Bugs

- A third greeting was recorded for Bassianus, but will never be heard in-game: *"Is it absolutely necessary for you to bother me right now?"*
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.5, fixes this bug.
- After moving to Riften, Bassianus was supposed to sleep at Haelga's Bunkhouse between 8pm and 4am. However, the sleep package never activates, causing him to wander Riften 24 hours a day.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Battle-Born Farm

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Wheat Mill.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Wheat_Mill.png) | Wheat Mill: Battle-Born Farm ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Battle-Born+Farm)) | | |

The Battle-Born Farm

**Battle-Born Farm** is a farm just outside [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), owned by the [Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle-Born "Skyrim:Battle-Born") clan who are influential in the city. [Alfhild](/wiki/Skyrim:Alfhild_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Alfhild Battle-Born") and [Gwendolyn](/wiki/Skyrim:Gwendolyn "Skyrim:Gwendolyn") tend the farm. The farm contains an [exterior](#Exterior) and a [farmhouse](#Battle-Born_Farm).

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Gwendolyn](/wiki/Skyrim:Gwendolyn "Skyrim:Gwendolyn") |

## Related Quests

- **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: Get paid to gather crops. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

The farm consists of several fields containing ten [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), five [gourds](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), and six bushels of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"). Alfhild will buy any leeks, gourds, or wheat you have. There is a [cow](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow "Skyrim:Cow") in a pen and three [chickens](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") wandering freely. The farm has lots of equipment around the property including a [grain mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Milling "Skyrim:Milling"), which is south of the house, a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), and a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") that are either side of the cow pen. There is also a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") which is under a covered store with a table and chair next to it and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") on the table. There are two [chicken nests](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") next to a walled field. There is a [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein"), two [corundum ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") to the north and one to the northeast, across the road from the property. There is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") among some rocks to the south as well. Around the house are several [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels and large vats, with a few flowering plants at the back of the house and along the roadside.

| Crops | Plants | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 5 [Gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd")  18 [Leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek")  6 [Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") | 2 [Lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender")  2 [Tundra Cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") | 3 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken")  1 [Cow](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow "Skyrim:Cow") | 2 [Chickens' Nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") |

### Battle-Born Farm

Inside Battle-Born Farm

The house is a single-room property with a stack of food barrels and sacks in the southwestern corner. Against the west wall is a narrow wooden table with a bowl of [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") on top. To the right, also against the west wall, is a bookcase holding eleven common books and a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"). In the southeastern corner is a square wooden table and two chairs, with an alcove to the left, along the east wall. The alcove serves as a bedroom and contains a double bed in the southeastern corner with an end table to the left holding a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") in a bowl. In the center of the room, toward the back, is a fire pit with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") over it. In the northwestern corner of the room is a cupboard holding several pieces of crockery, two bottles of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a [leathers strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), and a rack of [dog meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog_Meat "Skyrim:Dog Meat"). To the right of this is a food barrel with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") on top. Further along the north wall are a couple of wall shelves that hold a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), crockery, and a couple of food sacks. Against the east wall is a long wooden table and chairs, with a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a bowl of [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a bowl containing three [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), and a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"). There is an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie") by the hearth and a narrow wooden table against the partition wall between the bedroom and cooking areas. On this table is a bowl containing loaves of bread and crockery. There are also four [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") and two bunches of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear") hanging from a beam that supports the roof.

## Notes

- Though you can find and activate a [grain mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Milling "Skyrim:Milling") here, it will only lead to an animation, with no actual function in the game.
- The guard outside the farm will not be replaced should the Stormcloaks take Whiterun.
- All containers in the area, other than some barrels and sacks, are non-respawning and safe to store items in.
- Even if you help Alfhild Battle-Born, everything in the farmhouse may still be considered owned.
-  Version 2.1.1 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks the sacks, barrels, cow, pichfork, and bottles of wine outside the building as owned by the farm.

# Skyrim:Battle for Solitude

## Overview

The Stormcloaks mount their final offensive

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Get your orders from [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist").
2. Go to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") and listen to [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak")'s speech.
3. Fight your way to [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour").
4. Make [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") surrender.

### Assaulting the city

After taking [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad") and returning to [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist"), you will be told to meet [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") and help take [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). Make your way to the gates to Solitude to hear Ulfric's speech. After the speech, everyone will run into Solitude. Follow them in and fight your way to [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour"). If facing problems coping with the Imperial soldiers, it would be a good idea to stick with Ulfric. There will be several wooden barricades littering the city—three hits or less from a weapon or [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") spell will break them. The gate to the courtyard will be closed, so you will have to go around the city to get to Castle Dour.

### Negotiation at its finest

Once you've had enough fighting, enter Castle Dour. Galmar and Ulfric will appear inside with you. You will be put in a cutscene mode for a few seconds while Ulfric tells Galmar to secure the door. Head through the doorway with Galmar and Ulfric to confront [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") and [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke"). A lengthy dialogue commences, and despite Ulfric's pleas that she surrender, Rikke insists on standing her ground and engages in combat. Kill Rikke and beat Tullius into submission.

Once Rikke is dead and Tullius is on the floor, the fighting will stop, and a short conversation will occur. After some talking, Galmar and Ulfric will offer to give you the honor of finishing Tullius. Choose whether to accept their offer or decline and allow Ulfric to kill the General. If you choose to kill Tullius then Ulfric will give you a leveled sword with which to do the deed. If you decline then he will reward you with a leveled sword after he kills Tullius. This will complete the quest and begin the final stage of the [Liberation of Skyrim.](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim")

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked at the end of this quest:

-  **Hero of Skyrim** (30 points/Silver) — Capture [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") or [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm")

## Notes

- This quest, [Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)"), [Battle for Whiterun (Imperial)](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Imperial)"), and [Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm") are all different radiant versions of the same quest.
- The map marker for Solitude will disappear during the quest, so you will have to fast-travel to [Katla's Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Katla%27s_Farm "Skyrim:Katla's Farm") or some other nearby destination and walk from there to the gates of Solitude.
- To minimize game lag, bodies disappear soon after they have been killed.
- Even after you finish the quest, you'll still be able to craft Imperial armor at [blacksmith forges](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge").
- If you're currently doing the Dark Brotherhood quest [Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death"), the Battle for Solitude will be delayed until that quest is complete. Ulfric will stay in his palace, and if spoken to, will tell you, *"We're ready to march on Solitude, but the Emperor's cousin is getting married! If royal blood was spilt, all of Cyrodiil would be up in arms. We can't afford an all out war with the Empire. So we'll bide our time for now."*
- If you're currently doing Dark Brotherhood quests to assassinate the Emperor like [To Kill an Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:To_Kill_an_Empire "Skyrim:To Kill an Empire"), the Battle for Solitude will be delayed. After [The Battle for Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Hraggstad"), quest mark still remains on [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") and he says *"We're ready to launch our attack on Solitude. But the Emperor's visiting! We can't risk attacking now. So we'll bide our time."*
- If you complete this quest before finishing the main quest, you can [encounter](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke#Sovngarde "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") Legate Rikke in the mists of [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)").
- Finishing the quest will clear any bounty currently held by the player in the [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") Hold.
- After you finish the quest, the [Shrine of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrines") at the [Temple of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines") will be restored.
- Contrary to post-quest dialogue indicating that you can raid [Imperial Camps](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Imperial Camps") to further help the Stormcloaks, the commanders of these camps will still be marked as essential after the quest.
- Completing this quest will harm the relationship you have with outspoken Imperial supporters across Skyrim, giving you quite a number of hostile greetings. NPC functionality like trading or quest stages will not be affected though.

## Bugs

- After entering Castle Dour, you may get stuck in cutscene mode permanently without Ulfric or Galmar joining you. You can get arrested inside the East Empire Company Warehouse and then serve your time in jail. You can then access Castle Dour and Solitude. **?**
- When you're about to enter Solitude, you may get locked out of the city and say it requires a key to open the door, leaving you unable to finish the quest.
  -  Open the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console"), click on the door, and type `unlock`. The door will be unlocked and you can continue with the quest.
- The final confrontation with Legate Rikke and General Tullius is particularly buggy. Reports indicate a number of different things going wrong once you enter Castle Dour with Galmar and Ulfric, including:
  - Rikke and Tullius may leave combat mode. It is possible to carry on a conversation with General Tullius about how the war is going while Ulfric is standing right next to him with his axe drawn. It becomes impossible to end the quest.
  - Rikke may become invincible; attacking her until she has zero health will force her to the ground, but she will simply stand up moments later and recover full health. She is not always hostile upon standing up; it may be possible to hold a normal conversation without quest-specific dialogue.
    -  Opening the console and entering `setstage CWFinale 330` while Rikke, Ulfric, and Galmar are talking will progress to the next stage of the quest. Rikke and Tullius may still become hostile and need to be subdued after speaking however their deaths will no longer be required.
  - General Tullius may also become invincible, as the scripted conversation that results in his death may not be triggered by beating him to the ground. Although the "Talk to General Tullius" dialogue option may still appear, the option cannot be activated, and the quest cannot be completed as a result.
    - Striking Tullius with the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout may fix this.
    - One solution is to go complete the quest [The Fallen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fallen "Skyrim:The Fallen") and then complete 'The Battle for Solitude'.
    - Or simply reload a save from before this fight and redo the fight.
  - Tullius may be paralyzed accidentally when fighting is first initiated. He will fall to the ground as if dead, but proceed to talk and blink until Rikke is killed and Ulfric gives you the honor of killing him. Though he appears dead and cannot move, the slightest damage will kill him, allowing the quest to continue.
  - Additionally, you may find yourself permanently locked in the room with Rikke, Tullius, Galmar, and Ulfric, unable to leave as the only exit door requires a key that you don't have (and can't get anywhere within the room). The only option is reload an earlier save. **?**
- If you have a bounty in [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") and are caught by a guard prior to arrival at Solitude, you can submit to paying a fine and find yourself just outside Castle Dour, effectively skipping the entire battle.
- When you enter Solitude the city may be in its normal state with citizens and city guards wandering around instead of Imperial soldiers. This will cause guards to attack Ulfric, Galmar, and you if you attack guards in Castle Dour along with the [essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs") Legate. The quest can still be finished if you attack Ulfric. However, there will be no speech or cutscenes, and it is recommended that you leave the city soon after. Your bounty will not be reset until you fast travel somewhere else and then back to Solitude. **?**
- If you enter Solitude for the first time for this quest, you will find [Jaree-Ra](/wiki/Skyrim:Jaree-Ra "Skyrim:Jaree-Ra") casually standing around while the battle rages around him, waiting for you to speak to him so that he can start his [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!"). He is essential at this point, so he cannot be killed, but speaking to him will prevent you from defending yourself until you exit conversation with him. **?**
- If you enter the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace") during the battle, [Bolgeir Bearclaw](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolgeir_Bearclaw "Skyrim:Bolgeir Bearclaw") will have his weapon drawn, and [Elisif](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif "Skyrim:Elisif") will be in her quarters, making it impossible to talk to them. **?**
- If you have never visited Solitude prior to the battle, it can break this quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- If you have completed the quest [Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood! "Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!"), then once you have liberated Haafingar, Ulfric will respond, "We're ready to march on Solitude, but the Emperor's cousin is getting married." and the questline will not advance. **?**
- After killing General Tullius and Ulfric's second speech, Solitude may stay in war mode.
  - An easy solution is to fast travel to Windhelm and talk to Ulfric in the Palace of the Kings, where he will offer you to be Thane of Eastmarch. This should reset Solitude back to normal, with Stormcloak soldiers instead of Haafingar guards.
- After the battle, the covering over the well in the market topples over. This can block multiple characters' pathing.
- After the battle, the [Penitus Oculatus Outpost](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus_Outpost "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus Outpost") will remain active in [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge"), which can result in [Penitus Oculatus agents](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus") and Stormcloak soldiers engaging each other in combat.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, addresses this issue. If this quest and the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") questline are finished, the Penitus Oculatus Outpost will be cleared out.
- After the battle, Imperial soldiers can still be [randomly seen](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions "Skyrim:World Interactions") with Stormcloak prisoners, even though Tullius and Rikke are now dead meaning the Imperial soldiers won't have someone to report to anymore.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.0, addresses this issue. This random encounter will now be disabled once Solitude has fallen.

## Quest Stages

Only the quest stages and objectives that are possibly relevant to this radiant version of the quest are shown.

| Battle for Solitude (CWSiegeObj) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 1 |  | I am to join Ulfric Stormcloak in the final attack on Solitude, putting an end to the Imperial Legion in Skyrim, once and for all. |
| 8999 | ☒ |  |
| 9000 | ☑ | We have captured Solitude, killed General Tullius, and destroyed the final bastion of Imperial influence in Skyrim. |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 1000:* Get your Orders from Ulfric Stormcloak  *Objective 4002:* Force General Tullius to surrender  *Objective 4102:* Execute General Tullius [*verification needed — Are these the only three?*] |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 9999.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CWSiegeObj stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CWSiegeObj`.

# Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Imperial)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages.
