Forcing Ulfric Stormcloak to surrender

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Fight through waves of [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks").
2. Reach the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings").
3. Force [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") to surrender.

### For the Empire! For the Legion!

Arrive at [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") for the battle to begin. You will find [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") at the gates, giving a speech to a group of [Imperial Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier"):

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| *For the Empire! For the Legion!* | ***"All right. It's time to deliver the final blow to the Stormcloak rebellion. You have all fought bravely, and sacrificed much to bring us to this point. Ulfric thinks he can hide behind the walls of his castle. But we will fight our way in and drag him out through the rubble to face justice. Because this is the end for them, the Stormcloaks will fight like cornered rats. They will be fierce and crafty. But they are no match for Legionnaires. You are the best and the brightest warriors in Tamriel. Professional soldiers, fearless and devastating. The Emperor will be paying close attention to what happens here today. Men who distinguish themselves will be well rewarded. Ready now! Everyone, with me! For the Empire! For the Legion! Rrrrrraaaaaaaaaaaaahhhhhhh!!!!"*** |

When he finishes his speech, he and his soldiers will charge into the city. Follow them through the main gates.

### Battle for Windhelm

Once inside, you will be met by wave after wave of infinitely respawning [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") Soldiers. Your task now will be to fight your way through the opposition to reach the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings"). Debris will block the direct route to the palace, forcing you to find another way. After entering the city, take an immediate left and head west to the market square. Upon reaching the square, turn right past the blacksmith's [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") and travel north to the cemetery. Once there, take a left down the steps, then take the steps north past the [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Windhelm) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Windhelm)"). Upon reaching the top of the steps and smashing the barricade, march through Valunstrad and head east down the alley. Once you reach the end of the alley, turn left and head north up the steps, destroy the barricade, and proceed to the Palace of the Kings, where [Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") and his second in command, [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist"), are waiting for you.

### Palace of the Kings

When you enter the palace, Ulfric will be sitting on his throne with Galmar standing by his side. General Tullius and Legate Rikke will enter, and Tullius will demand Ulfric's surrender, stating that Ulfric is the only one standing between Skyrim and peace and that he needs to be killed to regain the peace. After they're done talking, Ulfric and Galmar will become hostile and attack the three of you. Kill Galmar and force Ulfric to his knees (Ulfric is still [essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs") at this point). If you are having trouble with this battle, you can allow Tullius and Rikke to do most of the fighting, as they are both essential. General Tullius will then prepare to kill Ulfric, but Ulfric will request that his death be at your hands. You will then be given the choice of executing Ulfric or making Tullius do it himself. If you choose to kill Ulfric, Tullius will hand you a leveled enchanted sword for the task, though you don't need to use the sword to kill Ulfric. If you choose to let the general kill Ulfric he will still give you the sword afterwards.

After Ulfric is dead, Tullius and Rikke will head outside. Follow them out and watch as Tullius gives a speech to the assembled Imperial soldiers, thanking them for their service.

After the completion of this quest, the Imperials will install a new Jarl, [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter"). If you later approach him, he will grant you the privilege of buying property in Windhelm and, if you speak to him, the opportunity to become [Thane of Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Eastmarch "Skyrim:Thane of Eastmarch").

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked at the end of this quest if you sided with the Imperials:

-  **Hero of Skyrim** (30 points/Silver) — Capture [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") or [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm")

- If you sided with the Stormcloaks, Windhelm is only the first step, and the achievement is instead obtained with the [Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude").

## Notes

- This quest, [Battle for Whiterun (Imperial)](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Imperial)"), [Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)") and [Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude") are all different radiant versions of the same quest.
- During and after the siege of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), three catapults are present in nearby [Windhelm Military Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Military_Camp "Skyrim:Windhelm Military Camp"). They can be activated to fire projectiles into Windhelm, though this has no effect on the siege.
- To minimize game lag, bodies disappear soon after they have been killed.
- If you complete this quest before finishing the main quest, you can encounter both [Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak#Sovngarde "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak")'s and [Galmar](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist#Sovngarde "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist")'s spirits in [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)"), lost in [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin")'s soul-ensnaring mist. Ulfric expresses dismay at how all his war did was feed Alduin, while Galmar is incensed that even in Sovngarde the Dragonborn still dogs his steps. After the defeat of Alduin, Galmar will state that an eternity is too long to hold a grudge and praise you for defeating Alduin.
- Finishing the quest will clear any bounty currently held by the player in [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch").
- Even after you finish the quest, the [Temple of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Talos "Skyrim:Temple of Talos") will remain free for Talos worship, and the [Shrine of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrines") there won't be removed.
- Contrary to post-quest dialogue indicating that you can raid [Stormcloak Camps](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") to further help the Legion, the commanders of these camps will still be marked as essential after the quest.
- Completing this quest will harm the relationship you have with outspoken Stormcloak supporters across Skyrim, giving you quite a number of hostile greetings. NPC functionality like trading or quest stages will not be affected though.

## Bugs

|  |
| --- |
| **To meet our site's higher standard of quality, this article or section may require cleanup.**  **The user who placed this here had the following concern:** There's an awful lot of guesswork here; needs cleanup To leave a message about the cleanup for this article, please add it to this article's [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Battle_for_Windhelm). |

- After killing Ulfric and Galmar, their corpses will not disappear and will remain in the palace permanently, even after Brunwulf has been made Jarl.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.

- If the Imperials take Windhelm when [Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice") is also active, the guard is never swapped out properly to allow the quest to be completed once the city has changed ownership.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, fixes this bug.

- After the Imperials take Windhelm, [Captain Lonely-Gale](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Lonely-Gale "Skyrim:Captain Lonely-Gale") is supposed to take over as steward but never does because [Jorleif](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorleif "Skyrim:Jorleif") is never exiled.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.

- After the battle is finished, Brunwulf Free-Winter may lack the "Jarl" prefix to his name when most other new Jarls get it automatically.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.

- After finishing the battle outside and entering the Jarl's palace, General Tullius will speak to Ulfric and initiate combat, but Ulfric and Galmar may ignore Legate Rikke and Tullius and attack only you, while the Legate and General simply draw their swords and watch. Both NPCs can then be forced into the recovery state but will not die, as they are still marked as essential.
  - This may be caused by advancing through the Civil War questline far enough that the [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") quest can't be started, resulting in Ulfric and Galmar mistakenly maintaining their essential status. Reload from before starting the battle and instead play through the rest of the main questline, or reload an earlier save that will allow you to complete the Season Unending quest. Alternatively, type `setstage MQ302 350` in console before entering the palace to mark Season Unending as completed.

- In some cases when you meet General Tullius outside of Windhelm, the city gates will be open slightly. If you activate the gates they will close and then lock. After this happens there will be no way to access Windhelm.
  - Reloading a previous save may only work if you go back before the start of the quest.
  -  This can be solved by opening the console, selecting the gate and using the "unlock" command.

- Sometimes after you hear General Tullius give his initial speech and charge into the Windhelm, the battle will not load. Instead you will enter the normal city with no Legion Soldiers or Stormcloaks. General Tullius and Legate Rikke will both be there and will attack the Windhelm guards on sight. If you have this bug, going back to a save before the start of the liberate Eastmarch quest will not help. What triggers this bug is currently unknown, but some unknown previous interaction with the city seems the probable culprit.
  -  You can use console commands to complete the quest, but Ulfric will continue to rule Windhelm and the house there will be inaccessible. A workaround to complete the quest with full imperial occupation of Eastmarch is to continue with General Tullius and [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") into the Palace, confront and defeat Ulfric, and then leave the city for thirty days until it resets.
  - This is possibly because General Tullius will follow his showdown scripting once you get him into the palace. When you enter the palace you need to move quickly away from the door or you will become stuck in cinematic mode. A solution to this issue is to quit without saving, and let the game pick up the auto save from inside the Palace of the Kings. This may take two or three attempts. The other thing you need to be careful about is the presence of two Windhelm guards at the door and [Yrsarald Thrice-Pierced](/wiki/Skyrim:Yrsarald_Thrice-Pierced "Skyrim:Yrsarald Thrice-Pierced"). The guards will attack General Tullius and Legate Rikke (who will not respond) and Yrsarald Thrice-Pierced will join the final battle, but since he is an essential character, you won't be able to kill him. Afterward, General Tullius will not give his speech and Yrsarald Thrice-Pierced will follow you around attacking until you leave the city. After the thirty days there should be no difference in result from a normal victory.

- After finishing the quest, Hadvar will constantly follow you with his sword drawn. This bug happens when he comes a few days after the battle to thank you.
  - To fix this, simply stand as close to him as possible, save your game, then close and relaunch Skyrim.

- After finishing [The Battle for Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Amol "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Amol") and returning to the Imperial camp, [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") tells you to get orders from [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius"), but the quest marker remains on Rikke.
  -  Open console and enter: `setstage CWSiegeObj 1`. This will start the siege quest.

- After finishing the quest, Brunwulf Free-Winter sometimes won't appear in the Palace of the Kings. All Stormcloak versions of the jarls and their housecarls will be there, sitting at the table, but without Brunwulf in the palace, you are unable to purchase Hjerim.
  -  Use the Unrelenting Force shout on everyone at the dinner table. This will give you a bounty in all the locations where the jarls were from. Fast travel away from Windhelm, then back.

- It is possible for the General to never give you his sword, forcing you to do the execution without it.

- After the battle ends, the game may continue looping the battle music, regardless of combat status.
  - Completely exiting the game and reloading will fix this.
  -  This can be fixed by opening the console and entering `removemusic MUScombatcivilwar`.

- If you talk to Rikke or Tullius after completing the quest, they'll tell you that they expect you to clear out any [Stormcloak camps](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") you come across. All occupants of these camps will continue to attack you after giving warnings to leave, but the Stormcloak commanders in each camp will still be marked as essential, so they will not be killable. Subsequently, camps cannot be cleared.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.3, addresses this issue. The commanders will no longer be essential at this point.
  -  Using the console, you can manually retrieve the base IDs of the commanders and set them to non-essential.

- If Ulfric is paralyzed when his health is depleted, he will remain on the ground and General Tullius won't kill him.
  - You can still kill Ulfric yourself, allowing the quest to continue.

- After Ulfric bleed out there is a chance that he is still essential **?**
  - To solve this problem `setstage D1444 330`.

## Quest Stages

Only the quest stages and objectives that are possibly relevant to this radiant version of the quest are shown.

# Skyrim:Battle of the Champions

## Overview

Face off against the other side's Champion

## Quick Walkthrough

1. *(if you have not yet chosen a side in the Civil War)* Read the [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_Champions "Skyrim:Battle of Champions") in [The Drunken Huntsman](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Drunken_Huntsman "Skyrim:The Drunken Huntsman"), then pass a Persuasion [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") check with [Legate Adventus Caesennius](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Adventus_Caesennius "Skyrim:Legate Adventus Caesennius") *or* give [snow bear pelts](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Snow Bear Pelt") or [Klija's Snow Bear Pelts](/wiki/Skyrim:Klija%27s_Snow_Bear_Pelts "Skyrim:Klija's Snow Bear Pelts") to [Yrsarald Thrice-Pierced](/wiki/Skyrim:Yrsarald_Thrice-Pierced "Skyrim:Yrsarald Thrice-Pierced").

:   :   *or*

1. *(if you have already chosen a side in the Civil War)* Wait for a letter from the Stormcloaks or the Legion (you may need to enter The Drunken Huntsman once to trigger the courier).
2. Speak to Adventus Caesennius or Yrsarald and loot all items from the nearby chest.
3. Make your way to the battlefield east of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") and kill all enemy soldiers. Loot the Champion's body to complete the quest.

### Become a Champion

You may have to take out the competition...

**Note: This stage of the quest is only available if you install the [Civil War Champions](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War_Champions "Skyrim:Civil War Champions") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") on a character that has not yet sided with the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") or the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks").**

Go to [The Drunken Huntsman](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Drunken_Huntsman "Skyrim:The Drunken Huntsman") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). On the counter inside, you will find a note called *[Battle of Champions](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_Champions "Skyrim:Battle of Champions")*, which describes an upcoming battle between the Legion and the Stormcloaks in the ongoing [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"). Both sides intend to nominate a Champion, but nobody has been chosen as of yet.

If you wish to side with the Legion, you must journey to [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") to speak with [Legate Adventus Caesennius](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Adventus_Caesennius "Skyrim:Legate Adventus Caesennius"). You can wear 3 imperial pieces(armor, boot and bracer, referring details to [Steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel "Skyrim:Steel")) to pose as an imperial soldier, if don't, you will have to pass a [Persuasion check (Speech 50)](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Average "Skyrim:Speech") to convince him to let you act as the Legion Champion. If your [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill is not particularly high, it would be wise to bring a [Fortify Persuasion](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Persuasion "Skyrim:Fortify Persuasion") potion with you. Once you persuade him, you will be handed the [Imperial Armory Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Armory_Key "Skyrim:Imperial Armory Key") to unlock a chest in the nearby equipment room.

If you instead wish to fight for the Stormcloaks, you must bring five [snow bear pelts](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Snow Bear Pelt") to [Yrsarald Thrice-Pierced](/wiki/Skyrim:Yrsarald_Thrice-Pierced "Skyrim:Yrsarald Thrice-Pierced") in the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). These can be taken from [snow bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Bear "Skyrim:Snow Bear") or purchased from hunters and general goods merchants starting at level 10, although at low levels you may have difficulty with this task. Luckily there is an alternative and more underhanded approach: the note mentions a prospective Champion named [Klija Wolf-Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Klija_Wolf-Claw "Skyrim:Klija Wolf-Claw") who wishes to fight for the Stormcloaks. She has already gathered the pelts and can be found at the small settlement of [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove") just south of Windhelm. She can be found at all hours at the [Steamscorch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Steamscorch_Mine "Skyrim:Steamscorch Mine") Camp and carries an item named [Klija's Snow Bear Pelts](/wiki/Skyrim:Klija%27s_Snow_Bear_Pelts "Skyrim:Klija's Snow Bear Pelts") on her person. It can be a challenge to [pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") the item from her, but be warned that killing her counts as murder and will land you with a significant [bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime#Bounties "Skyrim:Crime") if you are caught. Whichever way you go about obtaining enough pelts, speak with Yrsarald to receive the [Storm-Bear Chest Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm-Bear_Chest_Key "Skyrim:Storm-Bear Chest Key") unlocking a chest in the Palace's war room.

### Answer the Call

**Note: This stage of the quest is only available if you install the Creation on a character which has already joined the Legion or the Stormcloaks.**

If you're already a member of the Legion or the Stormcloaks, you will receive a letter by [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") [*verification needed — see [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Battle_of_the_Champions#Letter_from_the_Empire_.2F_Stormcloaks_when.3F)*] from your commanding officer, advising you that a challenge has been issued by the Stormcloaks and requesting your assistance in dealing with it. If you are a member of the Legion, you will receive a *[Letter from the Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_the_Empire "Skyrim:Letter from the Empire")* requesting that you speak with Legate Adventus Caesennius in Castle Dour to receive your custom forged equipment for this task. If you are a Stormcloak, you will instead receive a *[Letter from the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Letter from the Stormcloaks")* asking you to meet with Yrsarald Thrice-Pierced in the Palace of the Kings. Meet with your commanding officer to receive a key to a nearby chest.

### Prepare for Battle

Approach your fellow Champion

Whichever path you take, once you are named Champion you will need to unlock the relevant chest and loot every item within. The quest will not progress unless you take everything, so be sure to pick up both weapons even if you only mean to use one. The chest also contains the [Map of Battle Location](/wiki/Skyrim:Map_of_Battle_Location "Skyrim:Map of Battle Location"), which can be examined in your inventory if you wish. The quest marker will direct you to the battle location in any case, a clearing on the plains of [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") directly west of [Shimmermist Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Shimmermist_Cave "Skyrim:Shimmermist Cave"). When you arrive, you will find five soldiers from both sides facing off against each other, with the other Champion patiently waiting for you in the center. If you side with the Legion, the Champion will be Klija Wolf-Claw if you didn't steal her pelts, but if you stole her pelts you will face a generic [Stormcloak Champion](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Champion "Skyrim:Stormcloak Champion") instead. If you side with the Stormcloaks you will face a generic [Imperial Champion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Champion "Skyrim:Imperial Champion").

Speak with the other Champion to begin the battle. You will need to slaughter all enemy combatants and loot the fallen Champion for their gear in order to complete the quest. You may have issues with [encumbrance](/wiki/Skyrim:Encumbrance "Skyrim:Encumbrance") at this stage if you intend to bring all this equipment away with you. Both sets of items are extremely powerful and make for a worthy reward. After the completion of the quest, you will receive a *Letter of Commendation* (either the [Legion version](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_of_Commendation_(Imperial_Legion) "Skyrim:Letter of Commendation (Imperial Legion)") or [Stormcloak version](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_of_Commendation_(Stormcloak) "Skyrim:Letter of Commendation (Stormcloak)")) via courier from your commanding officer to congratulate you on your victory.

## Notes

- If you install Civil War Champions on a character who has already chosen a side in the Civil War, Klija Wolf-Claw will not appear at Kynesgrove.
- If you decide to steal Klija's pelts but side with the Legion anyway, you will face a generic [Stormcloak Champion](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Champion "Skyrim:Stormcloak Champion") at the battle.
- If over-encumberance occurs from taking the gear of both factions it would be helpful to have either Arvak or the Daedric horse to summon, mount and fast-travel away.
- [Bits and Pieces](/wiki/Skyrim:Bits_and_Pieces "Skyrim:Bits and Pieces") has a snow bear pelt on display that respawns every 10 days, making it easy to obtain the powerful Storm-Bear set even at level 1.
- Whichever side you choose, surviving soldiers will make their way to the inn in the capital and remain for a short time before you receive Letter of Commendation, Imperial soldiers to [The Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever"), Stormcloak soldiers to [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall").

## Bugs

- Yrsarald Thrice-Pierced will not actually take the five snow bear pelts from you if you choose to go that route.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6, fixes this bug.
- If Klija Wolf-Claw appears at Kynesgrove and you side with the Legion, two versions of her will exist at once. Killing her at the battle site will not disable the version at Kynesgrove. **?**
- After the associated armor is picked up, the game may crash.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.1130, fixes this bug.
- After the AE update patch, completing this quest can cause the following with great frequency: graphics issues, loading screens that fail to end, and crashes. Reloading a save before the battle portion of this quest can fix this, but completing the quest will cause it to happen again.
  - This bug may be fixed by storing the armor somewhere (i.e. a chest or display). It appears that being equipped or just in one's inventory (including companions) can cause these glitches.
  - Possible Fix (tested on PS5): Save after battle then loot gear. After first attempted fast travel from the battle site at end of battle, unending loading screen should occur. When this happens, close game and restart. Loot gear, then walk to a location in a new cell with item storage (like a home), Myrwatch is a verified working location. Store all items from this quest inside a container, then leave home and make new save. Close Skyrim and restart game. Associated bugs should stop, items should be retrievable and usable without further issue.
- After obtaining the Imperial Dragon Armor, the quest may fail to update, leaving you unable to progress.
  -  If this occurs, you can enter `setstage ccFFBSSE001_Quest 240` in the console to progress the quest.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccFFBSSE001_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccFFBSSE001_Quest`.

# Skyrim:Batum gra-Bar

## Overview

| Batum gra-Bar (RefID: 000955C0) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Bloated Man's Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloated_Man%27s_Grotto "Skyrim:Bloated Man's Grotto") | | |
| Race | [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") | Gender | Female |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000955C0 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000CE09C |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 0 (**Dead**) | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 25 |
| Voice Type | [FemaleOrc](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleOrc "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleOrc") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [DA05HuntersOfHircineFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DA05HuntersOfHircineFaction "Skyrim:DA05HuntersOfHircineFaction") | | |

Batum gra-Bar

**Batum gra-Bar** is a dead [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)"), and one of the hunters who shows up in [Bloated Man's Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloated_Man%27s_Grotto "Skyrim:Bloated Man's Grotto") hunting [Sinding](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinding "Skyrim:Sinding"). When you arrive, she is dead at the first campfire, presumably from wounds sustained fighting Sinding. She only spawns during the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Ill_Met_By_Moonlight "Skyrim:Ill Met By Moonlight").

She wears [hide armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor"), [hide bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers"), a [hide helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Helmet "Skyrim:Hide Helmet") and [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots"). She wields a leveled [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") and a leveled [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") with leveled [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows"), all of which may be up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") in quality at level 22. She also carries at least 25 gold.

## Related Quests

- **[Ill Met By Moonlight](/wiki/Skyrim:Ill_Met_By_Moonlight "Skyrim:Ill Met By Moonlight")**: Participate in the Daedric Prince [Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Hircine "Skyrim:Hircine")'s Great Hunt.

# Skyrim:Beast Stone

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Standing Stones.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Standing_Stones.png) | All-Maker Stone: Beast Stone ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Beast+Stone)) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 10 |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2StoneBeast | |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| West of [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall") East-southeast of the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak") | |

The Beast Stone

The **Beast Stone** is an [All-Maker Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:All-Maker_Stones "Skyrim:All-Maker Stones") west of [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall").

Once [cleansed](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones"), this stone gives you the power to [summon](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Werebear "Skyrim:Conjure Werebear") a [werebear](/wiki/Skyrim:Werebear "Skyrim:Werebear") to fight alongside you for 60 seconds. Once you use this power, it disappears from the Powers menu, and you must return to the Beast Stone to obtain it again.

## Related Quests

- **[Cleansing the Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones")**: Use the [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") to cleanse each of the remaining [All-Maker Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:All-Maker_Stones "Skyrim:All-Maker Stones").

## Walkthrough

The Thirsk warriors and the rieklings

The stone shows the usual signs of construction, with wooden scaffolding on the southeast side, and [pickaxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), [shovels](/wiki/Skyrim:Shovel "Skyrim:Shovel"), hammers, and carts in the vicinity. Several [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") plants and [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") grow around the stone. Paths lead southeast to Thirsk Mead Hall and west to the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak"), with a branching path leading north-northeast to the [Wind Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Wind_Stone "Skyrim:Wind Stone").

Before you cleanse the stone, a leveled [cultist](/wiki/Skyrim:Cultist "Skyrim:Cultist") will attack as you approach. During the day, two [rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling") will be working on and bowing to the stone. During the night, three more rieklings and [Elmus](/wiki/Skyrim:Elmus "Skyrim:Elmus") will also be found at the stone, and after you witness the dialogue between [Bujold the Unworthy](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold_the_Unworthy "Skyrim:Bujold the Unworthy") and [Kuvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Kuvar "Skyrim:Kuvar") at [Bujold's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Bujold's Retreat"), Bujold, [Halbarn Iron-Fur](/wiki/Skyrim:Halbarn_Iron-Fur "Skyrim:Halbarn Iron-Fur"), [Hilund](/wiki/Skyrim:Hilund "Skyrim:Hilund"), and Kuvar will be found here as well. When you cleanse the stone, a leveled [lurker](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker") will rise from the water around the base of the stone (or possibly appear on the nearby hill) and attack you and the workers. After the lurker is defeated, the rieklings will remain near the stone for a short time, then leave; however, if you linger for too long, they may eventually attack.

## Notes

- The Beast Stone also appears in *[Bloodmoon](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Beast_Stone "Bloodmoon:Beast Stone")*.

Beautiful Barbarian

The **Beautiful Barbarian** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(class) "Skyrim:Warrior (class)") and a possible assassination target during the recurring quest [The Dark Brotherhood Forever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dark_Brotherhood_Forever "Skyrim:The Dark Brotherhood Forever"). If chosen as the target, she will appear in the center of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"), just outside the [Vilemyr Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilemyr_Inn "Skyrim:Vilemyr Inn").

She wears a full set of [Stormcloak Officer Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Officer_Armor "Skyrim:Stormcloak Officer Armor") and wields a [steel greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Greatsword "Skyrim:Steel Greatsword").

## Related Quests

- **[The Dark Brotherhood Forever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dark_Brotherhood_Forever "Skyrim:The Dark Brotherhood Forever")**: Yet another child has prayed to their [mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother").

### The Dark Brotherhood Forever

Not knowing of her fate, she will ironically say to the player:

:   *"I'm dying for a rest. I swear, I could lie down right now, and just sleep forever."*

## Notes

- According to game data, she was originally meant to be found in the now nonexistent village of [Granite Hill](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard#Notes "Skyrim:Fort Sungard"), rather than Ivarstead.

## Bugs

- Sometimes the barbarian will appear with nothing equipped, despite having armor in her inventory.

# Skyrim:Beem-Ja

## Overview

| Beem-Ja (RefID: FF001022) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Ironbind Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironbind_Barrow "Skyrim:Ironbind Barrow") | | |
| Race | [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") | Gender | Male |
| Level | PC×1.2 (range=5-30) | Class | [Sorcerer](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorcerer "Skyrim:Sorcerer") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | FF001022 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0006CD5B |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 50+(PC-0.8)×10 | | |
| [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 150+(PC-0.8)×6 | | |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 40+(PC-0.8)×2 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction")**, **[Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion")**, [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor"), [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") | | |

| Voice Type | [MaleArgonian](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleArgonian "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleArgonian") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [Adventurers](/wiki/Skyrim:Adventurers "Skyrim:Adventurers") | | |

Beem-Ja relaxing with a drink

**Beem-Ja** is an [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") [sorcerer](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatSorcerer "Skyrim:CombatSorcerer") who sits at a small make-shift campsite just outside of [Ironbind Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironbind_Barrow "Skyrim:Ironbind Barrow") alongside his adventuring partner, the [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [Salma](/wiki/Skyrim:Salma "Skyrim:Salma").

Beem-Ja wears [blue mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Blue Mage Robes"), [gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000261c1 "Skyrim:Clothing"), [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0006b46c "Skyrim:Clothing"), and a [leveled](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Items "Skyrim:Leveled Items") enchanted [ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring "Skyrim:Ring"). He carries four [torches](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch"), a leveled [staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Staves "Skyrim:Staves"), a leveled enchanted [circlet](/wiki/Skyrim:Circlet "Skyrim:Circlet") of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction"), the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Frostfall, v10](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Frostfall,_v10 "Skyrim:2920, Frostfall, v10")*, a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_to_Beem-Ja "Skyrim:Letter to Beem-Ja") from Salma's father, and a small amount of gold.

## Related Quests

- **[Coming of Age](/wiki/Skyrim:Coming_of_Age "Skyrim:Coming of Age")**: Help a [daring adventurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Salma "Skyrim:Salma") and her companion retrieve their riches.

## Quest-Related Events

As you arrive at Ironbind Barrow, you will notice Beem-Ja and Salma at their campsite and overhear them argue about whether to enter the barrow.

:   **Salma:** *"How can you just sit here and wait? We should be in there!"*
:   **Beem-Ja:** *"We must gather our strength. Who knows what's inside?"*
:   **Salma:** *"Treasure, that's what! Get off your scaly rump and let's go."*
:   **Beem-Ja:** *"Hush, Salma. We aren't alone."*

If you approach him after this conversation, he'll direct you to talk to Salma and express frustration.

:   *"Speak with Miss Salma, if you wish to speak."*
:   *"I grow tired of debating this. If Miss Salma insists on this folly, so be it."*
:   *"I admit, there is strength in numbers. Perhaps between us..."*

After telling Salma that you plan on entering the barrow, Beem-Ja and Salma will run into the barrow with you.

If you attempt to talk to him while in the barrow, he will say:

:   *"We're in this together. Stay close."*
:   *"This is no time for idle talk."*
:   *"Not now. Stay alert."*

Once you clear out the spiders in the ice caves and approach the tomb, he will say:

:   *"This is it. We've found [Gathrik's](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlord_Gathrik "Skyrim:Warlord Gathrik") tomb."*

As you approach the closed gate ahead, he will say:

:   *"Well? There must be a way through. Look around."*

After you progress further through the tomb and enter a hallway with a helmet on a pedestal, he will caution you:

:   *"Don't rush ahead. This is a trap if I ever saw one."*

As you get close to the final chamber, Beem-Ja will continue to reveal suspicious knowledge about the barrow.

:   **Beem-Ja:** *"This is it! Gathrik awaits us!"*
:   **Salma:** *"What are you on about? Let's just get the treasure here and go."*

After Gathrik is defeated, Beem-Ja will run up to you and reveal his true colors:

:   *"Fool. I should thank you. I knew the girl wouldn't be strong enough to help me kill Gathrik alone.
    There's just one more thing I need from you. To fully absorb Gathrik's power I require a blood sacrifice.
    Your blood should be good enough. This will go easier for us both if you don't bother fighting back."*

He will then proceed to attack you and you will have no choice but to kill him.

## Notes

- The letter from Salma's father implies that Beem-Ja is in service to Salma's family.
- After he becomes aggressive, sheathing your weapons may cause Beem-Ja to become non-aggressive again. Gathrik's corpse will remain floating in the air surrounded by magic, and Salma does not disappear upon leaving the barrow. Instead Salma and Beem-Ja will return to the entrance of the area where you first found them. Salma is permanently aggressive towards Beem-Ja, however, and will attack him on sight.
- Attacking Beem-Ja before he is aggressive will cause Salma to attack you.
- The base game version of Oblivion's *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_IV:_Oblivion_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls IV: Oblivion Official Game Guide")* mentions "Beem-Ja" under the male Argonian "Sample Names For Tamriel's Races".

## Bugs

- Beem-Ja may equip the circlet he carries, and as he carries no other clothes or armor, his robes will be removed as they need a head slot. This results in him appearing naked.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Before the Storm

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Main.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Main.png) | **Inform the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") about the dragon attack on [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar") or [Ralof](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralof "Skyrim:Ralof") |
| Location(s): | [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"), [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") |
| Reward: | Leveled Armor |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 (Balgruuf) =1 (Alvor or Gerdur) |
| ID: | MQ102 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound") | **Next →** [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound") | | → Next | [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)") | | |

[Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin") flying over [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(place) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (place)")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. *(Optional)* Speak to [Alvor](/wiki/Skyrim:Alvor "Skyrim:Alvor") or [Gerdur](/wiki/Skyrim:Gerdur "Skyrim:Gerdur") in [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood").
2. Go to [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
3. Seek out Jarl [Balgruuf the Greater](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater").

### First Steps

*"That place always used to give me nightmares."*

*"See that ruin up there? Bleak Falls Barrow."*

As you head out from the dungeon with either [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar") or [Ralof](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralof "Skyrim:Ralof"), the dragon that attacked [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") will travel over your head. Hadvar or Ralof will advise you to get down, but you're free to stand up and watch the dragon fly away. Hadvar or Ralof will comment on the dragon and continue on the path. You can now explore the area and advance to [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood") at your own pace or follow whoever is accompanying you down the path. Following Hadvar or Ralof does not grant any special bonuses, but you do get to listen to your companion comment on the world around you, and they will point out the [Guardian Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Guardian_Stones "Skyrim:The Guardian Stones") and let you pick one that suits you. He will comment differently depending which stone you choose.

|  |
| --- |
| - The Warrior Stone (Hadvar): *"Warrior, good! I knew you shouldn't have been on that cart the minute I laid eyes on you."* - The Warrior Stone (Ralof): *"Warrior, good! Those stars will guide you to honor and glory."* - The Mage Stone: *"Mage, eh? Well, to each his own. It's not for me to judge."* - The Thief Stone: *"Thief, eh? It's never too late to take charge of your own fate, you know."* |

### A Friend of a Friend

Hadvar recounting the events at Helgen to Alvor's family

Ralof telling Gerdur and Hod what happened in Helgen

Once you arrive at the village of [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"), you will be directed to speak to [Alvor](/wiki/Skyrim:Alvor "Skyrim:Alvor"), the local smith (if you chose to follow [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar") during the flight from Helgen) or [Gerdur](/wiki/Skyrim:Gerdur "Skyrim:Gerdur"), the woodmill owner (if you chose to follow [Ralof](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralof "Skyrim:Ralof")). Explain your situation and he or she will recommend you seek out the jarl of the region, Jarl [Balgruuf the Greater](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") at his [palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). They will also offer you what assistance they can (in the form of some low level food, potions, and jewelry) to get you started. Only Gerdur will give a key to her house.

If you arrive in Riverwood very late, then the person you're directed to meet won't immediately offer you assistance. If you ask whether you can take any supplies, you will be allowed to take some things, and be directed to see the jarl.

### To Whiterun

Head out over the bridge out of town and follow the path north to [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). Upon arrival at the main gate, a guard will tell you the city is closed to visitors. Any one of the dialogue options you are presented with will have him let you in the city, except for trying to intimidate the guard. Once inside, follow the path up to [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") and enter. When you approach Jarl Balgruuf, his housecarl, [Irileth](/wiki/Skyrim:Irileth "Skyrim:Irileth"), will ask you why you are interrupting the meeting; any dialogue option will gain you an audience. Speak with Jarl Balgruuf to complete the quest and begin the next. He will reward you with a piece of leveled armor. Whether you receive light or heavy is governed by your aptitude in those skills. If they are equal, Balgruuf will give you heavy armor.

## Notes

- If you accompanied Hadvar out of Helgen, you will have free access to the low-value items at Alvor's smithy, including the stacks of ingots (useful for learning smithing), and also the low-value items inside [their house](/wiki/Skyrim:Alvor_and_Sigrid%27s_House "Skyrim:Alvor and Sigrid's House"). If you accompanied Ralof, you will be given a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Gerdur%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Gerdur's House") to [Hod and Gerdur's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Hod_and_Gerdur%27s_House "Skyrim:Hod and Gerdur's House"), and be able to take low-value items inside.
- No matter what choice you have made, you can also barter with Alvor and [help him](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmithing_Tutorial "Skyrim:Blacksmithing Tutorial") around his shop for some [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") experience, and Gerdur's husband [Hod](/wiki/Skyrim:Hod "Skyrim:Hod") will [pay](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood") you for any firewood.
- It is possible to become friends with both Alvor and Hod during this quest. The first thing you need to do is to side with Hadvar during Unbound, then escort him to Riverwood and talk to Alvor. After that, your final step is to sell firewood to Hod. If done correctly, both men will treat you as a friend before the quest is finished.
- You can talk to Hadvar or Ralof (depending on who you sided with) on the way to Riverwood and ask them about various topics, including dragons, Ulfric Stormcloak, the war, Talos worship, and how to join their respective sides.
- Meeting with Alvor or Gerdur is completely optional as they only direct you to Whiterun and offer you a few items.
  - If Alvor or Gerdur die before you speak with them, the objective "Talk to Alvor"/"Talk to Gerdur" will fail; however the quest can be continued by visiting Dragonsreach as normal.
- Progressing to Stage 30 of this quest ("Talk to the Jarl of Whiterun") is a trigger to enable [Falkreath Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Falkreath Stormcloak Camp") if all other required conditions are met.
- Once Alvor or Gerdur are spoken to, you'll be able to freely search the barrels inside [Sleeping Giant Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Giant_Inn "Skyrim:Sleeping Giant Inn") and use the double bed in Helgen.
- While on your way to Whiterun, you may encounter some of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") fighting a giant. [Aela the Huntress](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress") will approach you once the fight is finished.
- With version 3.0.1 of the [Unofficial Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), the Whiterun Guard will no longer perform endless forcegreets if you decide to "come back later" when trying to enter Whiterun.
- It is possible to enter Whiterun without ever speaking to the gate guard who stops the player by pick-pocketing the key from him, although it is very difficult to get into pick-pocket range without ever speaking to him.
  - The most consistent way to prevent talking to the guard is to pick-pocket him from behind the gate in out-of-bounds Whiterun, which happens to also be the fastest way to enter Whiterun during this quest.
- After you finish the quest, 3 Whiterun Guards will be present in Riverwood. The pile of logs outside of Riverwood will also be converted into a campfire with two bed rolls and a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking").

## Bugs

- Sometimes Gerdur will not have an option to ask about the dragon, causing the main quest to be frozen.
  - Ask Alvor for supplies. After you look through his inventory, he will start by saying *"The Jarl needs to know if there's a dragon on the loose. Riverwood is defenseless..."* Listen to him speak and he will mention that you should inform [the jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater"). After that, the quest will update.
- Similarly, Alvor may not have an option about the dragon, and the quest will not be able to progress.
  - Go to [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") and talk to the jarl to advance the quest.
- The real time timer for entering Alvor's home to trigger the scene is very short, potentially causing the overall scene to fail.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.0, fixes this bug.
  - Talk to Alvor to continue the quest regularly. The scene is skipped.
- The double bed in the destroyed Helgen inn is considered "owned" when you start the quest.
  - Escaping with Hadvar and becoming friends with his uncle Alvor (by speaking with him or finishing the quest) should allow you to use it properly.
- If you go straight to [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") and speak to [Jarl Balgruuf](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater"), despite never meeting [Alvor](/wiki/Skyrim:Alvor "Skyrim:Alvor"), you still have the dialogue option as you spoke to him. **?**

## Quest Stages

| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |

|  | Ralof suggested that we head to the nearby town of Riverwood. His sister owns a lumbermill there and should be able to help us. |
| 30 |  | Hadvar's uncle Alvor asked me to take word to the Jarl of Whiterun of the dragon attack on Helgen, and to ask the Jarl to send soldiers to protect Riverwood. *Objective 30:* Talk to the Jarl of Whiterun |
|  | Ralof's sister Gerdur asked me to take word to the Jarl of Whiterun of the dragon attack on Helgen, and to ask the Jarl to send soldiers to protect Riverwood. *Objective 30:* Talk to the Jarl of Whiterun |

| 160 | ☑ | Hadvar's uncle Alvor asked me to take word to the Jarl of Whiterun of the dragon attack on Helgen, and to ask the Jarl to send soldiers to protect Riverwood. I delivered the news to Jarl Balgruuf in Whiterun, and he rewarded me for my help. |
| ☑ | Ralof's sister Gerdur asked me to take word to the Jarl of Whiterun of the dragon attack on Helgen, and to ask the Jarl to send soldiers to protect Riverwood. I delivered the news to Jarl Balgruuf in Whiterun, and he rewarded me for my help. |
| ☑ | When I arrived in Whiterun, I told the Jarl about the dragon attack on Helgen, and he rewarded me for my efforts. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 2, 5, 12, 14, 15, 17, 22, 23, 25, 26, 50, 60, 75, 80, 82, 85, 90, 150, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MQ102 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MQ102`.

## Overview

Beggar

This Beggar is an [elder](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder "Skyrim:Elder") found at the [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") docks as part of the related quest. Unlike most [beggars](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggars "Skyrim:Beggars"), he will not give you a [blessing in return for 1 gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_all_Beggars_Have "Skyrim:Quest all Beggars Have").

### Heart of Crimson

:   **Here. Have a hundred gold pieces. (100 gold)**

:   **Here. Have a gold piece. (1 gold)**

:   **Instead of alms, I will pray for your prosperity.**

:   **You look hungry. Here, have some bread.**

    :   *"Thank you, oh thank you."*

# Skyrim:Beggar's Row

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Beggar's Row ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Beggar%27s+Row)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[A Dance in Fire, v7](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v7 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v7")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| RiftenBeggarsRow | |
| Region | |
| [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | |
| Location | |
| [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | |
| Special Features | |
| [Shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") | [Empty](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Empty") Empty |

Part of Beggar's Row

**Beggar's Row** is a small part of a sewer that has been converted into a homeless den in lower [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), by the canal that runs through the center of the city. It is by the northern stairs down from upper Riften, opposite [Elgrim's Elixirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim%27s_Elixirs "Skyrim:Elgrim's Elixirs"). It only contains one [interior zone](#Beggar.27s_Row).

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Edda](/wiki/Skyrim:Edda "Skyrim:Edda")  [Madesi](/wiki/Skyrim:Madesi "Skyrim:Madesi") [Jeweler](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Jeweler")  [Snilf](/wiki/Skyrim:Snilf "Skyrim:Snilf") |

## Beggar's Row

Outside the door are several barrels that are free to take from. Beggar's Row is a heavily vaulted part of the sewer, that has two owned hay piles and one owned bedroll inside it. [Madesi](/wiki/Skyrim:Madesi "Skyrim:Madesi"), [Edda](/wiki/Skyrim:Edda "Skyrim:Edda") and [Snilf](/wiki/Skyrim:Snilf "Skyrim:Snilf") all sleep in here at night. There is a campfire to the north and a couple of chairs as well as several [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks and barrels around the place. Scattered about the floor are a couple of bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and various vegetables, a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg") and several pieces of cheese. At the southwest connection there are two bottles of [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma"). There is a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[A Dance in Fire, v7](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v7 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v7")* due north upon entering, under a fern. The flat sack near the tipped-over basket is non-respawning, while the other upright sack does respawn.

## Notes

- There is an  "Empty") Empty [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") on the right door step before the entrance.

# Skyrim:Beggars

## Overview

This article is about NPC beggars. For other uses, see [Beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggar "Skyrim:Beggar").

There are a number of **beggars** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"). The majority of them will [ask for a gold piece](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_all_Beggars_Have "Skyrim:Quest all Beggars Have") when approached; giving them one gold will reward you with the blessing [The Gift of Charity](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gift_of_Charity "Skyrim:The Gift of Charity").

| Name | Location | Gift of Charity |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [Angrenor Once-Honored](/wiki/Skyrim:Angrenor_Once-Honored "Skyrim:Angrenor Once-Honored") | [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall") ([Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm")) | Yes |
| [Beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggar_(person) "Skyrim:Beggar (person)") ([CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Ebony_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Ebony Plate")) | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") docks | No |
| [Brenuin](/wiki/Skyrim:Brenuin "Skyrim:Brenuin") | [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare") ([Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")) | Yes |
| [Degaine](/wiki/Skyrim:Degaine "Skyrim:Degaine") | [The Warrens](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrens "Skyrim:The Warrens") ([Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth")) | Yes |
| [Dervenin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dervenin "Skyrim:Dervenin") | [Temple of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines") ([Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude")) | Yes |
| [Edda](/wiki/Skyrim:Edda "Skyrim:Edda") | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | Yes |
| [Lucia](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucia "Skyrim:Lucia") ([HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")) | Wind District ([Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")) | Yes |
| [Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Narfi "Skyrim:Narfi") | [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") ([The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift")) | Yes |

| [Svari](/wiki/Skyrim:Svari "Skyrim:Svari") | [Addvar's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvar%27s_House "Skyrim:Addvar's House") ([Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude")) | Yes |

## Related Quests

- **[Argonian Ale Extraction](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Ale_Extraction "Skyrim:Argonian Ale Extraction")**: [Brenuin](/wiki/Skyrim:Brenuin "Skyrim:Brenuin") longs for the taste of [Argonian Ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Ale "Skyrim:Argonian Ale"). Can you steal some for him?
- **[Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice")**: [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") is plagued by a shadowy killer.
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Gray Cowl of Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_of_Nocturnal "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl of Nocturnal")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_Returns! "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl Returns!"): Investigate the legend of the Gray Fox.
- **[Heart of Crimson](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_of_Crimson "Skyrim:Heart of Crimson")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Ebony_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Ebony Plate"): Confront the murderous leader of a bandit gang.
- **[The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella")**: Find a new [Sybil](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra") for the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella").
- **[Kill Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Narfi "Skyrim:Kill Narfi")**: Kill a hapless [beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Narfi "Skyrim:Narfi") in [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead").
- **[The Mind of Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_Madness "Skyrim:The Mind of Madness")**: Gain access to and solve the mystery of the [Pelagius Wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_Wing "Skyrim:Pelagius Wing").
- **[Quest all Beggars Have](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_all_Beggars_Have "Skyrim:Quest all Beggars Have")**: Take pity on a beggar. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Speak to Degaine](/wiki/Skyrim:Speak_to_Degaine "Skyrim:Speak to Degaine")**: Ask a [beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Degaine "Skyrim:Degaine") about money.
- **[The Straw that Broke](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Straw_that_Broke "Skyrim:The Straw that Broke")**: Discover what is plaguing [Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Narfi "Skyrim:Narfi")'s mind.

| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| [Essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs") | Yes, until [Get Outfitted](/wiki/Skyrim:Get_Outfitted "Skyrim:Get Outfitted") is complete. | | |
| Voice Type | [MaleNord](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleNord "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleNord") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionHaafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionHaafingar "Skyrim:CrimeFactionHaafingar"); [ServicesSolitudeBlacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:ServicesSolitudeBlacksmith "Skyrim:ServicesSolitudeBlacksmith"); [SolitudeBitsAndPiecesFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:SolitudeBitsAndPiecesFaction "Skyrim:SolitudeBitsAndPiecesFaction"); [SolitudeBlacksmithFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:SolitudeBlacksmithFaction "Skyrim:SolitudeBlacksmithFaction"); [TownSolitudeFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownSolitudeFaction "Skyrim:TownSolitudeFaction") | | |

Beirand

**Beirand** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:VendorBlacksmith "Skyrim:VendorBlacksmith") who runs the [smithy](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Blacksmith "Skyrim:Solitude Blacksmith") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") with the help of his assistant, [Heimvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimvar "Skyrim:Heimvar"). He will [give you](/wiki/Skyrim:Get_Outfitted "Skyrim:Get Outfitted") Imperial armor after [joining the legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Legion "Skyrim:Joining the Legion"). He is married to [Sayma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sayma "Skyrim:Sayma") and has one son, [Kayd](/wiki/Skyrim:Kayd "Skyrim:Kayd").

When you first enter Solitude, Beirand will be attending [Roggvir's](/wiki/Skyrim:Roggvir "Skyrim:Roggvir") execution. Before it takes place, he will only say, *"I've been waiting for Roggvir's execution. Talk to me later."* Once Roggvir dies, he will comment, *"A traitor right up to the end."* and tell you, *"He died well."*

After the execution, he will resume his schedule: between 8am and 10pm, he can be found working at the smithy. He then spends two hours at [home](/wiki/Skyrim:Bits_and_Pieces "Skyrim:Bits and Pieces") with his family, chatting, relaxing, taking a nap, or having a bite. He goes to bed at midnight.

Beirand wears a [blacksmith's apron](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith%27s_Apron#0005b69f "Skyrim:Blacksmith's Apron") along with a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes#0005b69e "Skyrim:Shoes"). He carries his [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Solitude_Blacksmith "Skyrim:Key to Solitude Blacksmith") to the Solitude Blacksmith, a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Bits_and_Pieces "Skyrim:Key to Bits and Pieces") to his wife's store, Bits and Pieces, a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"), and a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). In combat, he relies on a [steel mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Steel Mace").

## Related Quests

- **[Get Outfitted](/wiki/Skyrim:Get_Outfitted "Skyrim:Get Outfitted")**: Get a free set of Imperial armor.

### Get Outfitted

If you have just joined the Imperial Legion, you will be sent to Beirand to [get outfitted](/wiki/Skyrim:Get_Outfitted "Skyrim:Get Outfitted"):

:   **General Tullius said you'd get me outfitted.**
:   *"Yep. I have just one question for you. Light, medium, or heavy?"*
:   **What?**
:   *"Light armor for scouting detail, heavy armor for full on combat, or something in between?"*

:   **Light**

    :   *"Alright... here you go. Should keep you light on your feet, and hold up decent enough if you wind up trading blows with the enemy."*

:   **Medium**

    :   *"Alright. This here's enough to keep your insides from spilling out, except from the fiercest of blows, and shouldn't weigh you down too much."*

:   **Heavy**

    :   *"They don't make finer steel anywhere else. If this doesn't keep you from dying, nothing will."*

Whichever set of armor you chose, he will end with:

:   *"Now, that's it. One free outfit per soldier. You lose that, or get it banged up, you'll need to pay like everyone else."*

## Dialogue

While he is working at the forge, he will advertise his goods to potential customers, shouting:

:   *"I've got weapons for givin', and armor for gettin'!"*
:   *"Arms and armor! Forged by a master craftsman!"*
:   *"I got some fine armor, if you're lookin'."*
:   *"Need a weapon? Hmmm... By the looks of ya, yeah... Think I've got somethin' you can use."*
:   *"It's good to be away from the forge for a bit."*

Should you approach him for conversation, he will comment:

:   *"Wanderer like you must have plenty of tales to tell. But I'm afraid I'm too busy to hear 'em."*

Depending on who controls Solitude, he will also remark on his seemingly endless job:

:   *"Seems there's no end to the needs of the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). But what can I help you with?"*
:   *"When the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") took Solitude, I thought for sure things would slow down. But they keep me just as busy as the Imperials."*

When you bid him farewell, he will tell you:

:   *"Return anytime you need arms or armor. My forge never rests."*
:   *"Keep safe. And always wear your armor."*

If you offer to invest in his business:

:   **I'd like to make an investment in your business.**
:   *"Such an investment will mean that I can take better care of my family, as well as my customers."*
:   **Let's see what you can do with this.**
:   *"You'll look back on this as one of your best decisions, I swear it."*

When spoken to directly he can be asked questions about himself and his work:

:   **Have you considered getting out there and fighting?**
:   *"I think I would, if it weren't for my son. And my wife.
    Oh, Sayma would have my hide if I even suggested I might step foot on a battlefield. You think Stormcloaks and Legionnaires are dangerous? Ha!"*

You can also ask him about his job as an armorer. If the Imperial Legion controls Solitude:

:   **You make armor for the Imperials?**
:   *"It's almost all I have time for these days. The men training here in Solitude and the troops out in the field, they all need weapons and armor."*

If you have not joined the Imperials, he will end by suggesting:

:   *"You should look into joining. They could use every hand they can get."*

If you have already, he will instead say:

:   *"But I'm not telling you anything you don't already know."*

Either way, you can ask him if he is dedicated to the Empire:

:   **You're pretty dedicated to the Empire, then?**
:   *"Ah... To be honest, no. But [High King Torygg](/wiki/Skyrim:High_King_Torygg "Skyrim:High King Torygg") supported them, and now her lady [Elisif](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair") has thrown in with them. You could say I'm a King's man at heart. Hmph. I guess that's 'Jarl's man' now. My loyalty lies with Solitude. So where Jarl Elisif leads, I follow."*

If the Stormcloaks have seized the city, you can instead ask him:

:   **So you make armor for the Stormcloaks?**
:   *"These days? Aye. Most of what I make is for folk like you. There's still Imperial camps to be cleaned up, as you know. And that takes arms and armor."*

## Conversations

While at work, he will jest with his apprentice Heimvar:

**Beirand**: *"Come on, Heimvar. My son could stoke the forge better than you do!"* **OR** *"You're making progress, Heimvar. But my boy could still work the bellows better than you do!"*
**Heimvar**: *"Yeah, but can he hammer the anvil for 8 hours straight?"* **OR** *"Sure, but I bet he can't hold his mead as well as me!"*
**Beirand**: *"Give him time. In a couple years, he'll be the age you were when you started!"* **OR** *"Right you are! Guess I'll keep training you... for now."*

At Bits and Pieces, Sayma will talk to either Beirand or Kayd:

**Sayma**: *"Sure has been quiet around the shop lately."* **OR** *"We hardly ever get new customers anymore."*
**Sayma**: *"Not that I mind the break, of course. But, still..."* **OR** *"I suppose in wartime, people aren't looking to part with their old junk..."*
**Beirand**: *"We'll make it through, dear. We always do."* **OR** *"It's okay, dear. More work than ever down at the blacksmith."*
**OR** **Kayd**: *"Who needs customers and their old junk?"* **OR** *"Father oughtta punch them in the mouth! That'd get people in here!"*

## Notes

- Although Beirand tells you that you'll need to pay if you lose or damage the Imperial armor set he gave you in Get Outfitted, you can forge a new set yourself.
  - [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch") 1.9 makes it possible to forge Imperial Light Armor.

## Bugs

- Beirand may die when the ground under his feet unloads when you visit the Blue Palace.
  - Never finishing [Get Outfitted](/wiki/Skyrim:Get_Outfitted "Skyrim:Get Outfitted") will keep Beirand as essential and prevent him from dying from any cause.
  -  Beirand can be set to essential using `setessential 00013261 1`. Do this immediately after finishing [Get Outfitted](/wiki/Skyrim:Get_Outfitted "Skyrim:Get Outfitted") so his essential status is not wiped.
- If you join the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") (either [initially](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Joining the Stormcloaks") or by defecting after [The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown (Imperial)")), the quest where you can pick up free Imperial gear is never shut down which leaves Beirand in a perpetual essential alias.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, fixes this bug.

Beitild's House

**Beitild's House** is the house owned by [Beitild](/wiki/Skyrim:Beitild "Skyrim:Beitild") in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").

It is located near the docks, between [Silus Vesuius's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Silus_Vesuius%27s_House "Skyrim:Silus Vesuius's House") and [the Mortar and Pestle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mortar_and_Pestle "Skyrim:The Mortar and Pestle"). It only contains one [interior zone](#Beitild.27s_House).

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Beitild](/wiki/Skyrim:Beitild "Skyrim:Beitild") |

## Related Quests

- **[Kill Beitild](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Beitild "Skyrim:Kill Beitild")**: Resolve a feud in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").

### Exterior

There are steps leading up to a porch at the front of the house. To the right of the door are two barrels containing [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"). There are several piles of firewood on the left side of the porch, and a wooden bench on the right. The house faces the bay and is protected by a novice lock.

### Beitild's House

Beitild's house

The house is a simple single-room dwelling where [Beitild](/wiki/Skyrim:Beitild "Skyrim:Beitild") sleeps at night. She carries a copy of the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Beitild%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Beitild's House") to the house. It contains typical furnishings. There is a square table with a chair in the western corner of the house with two medium [coin purses](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and five loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") placed on top. Coming out of the middle of the northwest wall is a large double bed, with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the end containing leveled items. To the right of the bed is a round wooden table holding a basket containing three [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg").

In the middle of the northeast wall is a fireplace and [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"), a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword") on the mantlepiece, and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes "Skyrim:Shoes") in front of the hearth. To the left of the fireplace, against the northeast wall, is a wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"). To the right is a long wooden table and bench. On the table is a bottle of alto wine, a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), a [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), and an [Eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"). Under the table is a [potion of vigor](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Vigor "Skyrim:Potion of Vigor").

Opposite the table, against the southwest wall, is a set of shelves holding two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulb, three potatoes, four bottles of wine, two bottles of alto wine, and several pieces of cheese on top. Above the shelves are two garlic braids, three bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). To the left is a basket on the floor containing two leeks, and to the right is a food barrel.

## Notes

- The *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* describes the building as follows:

:   *"Beitild Iron-Breaker manages Iron-Breaker Mine. She's in constant competition with Leigelf Quicksilver, the owner of Quicksilver Mine and her former husband. Beitild lives in the house she used to share with her husband. She refuses to do much else but tend to her mine, eat, and sleep."*

- Other than some barrels and sacks, all containers in the area are non-respawning and safe to store items in if you wish.

# Skyrim:Beitild

## Overview

| Beitild (RefID: 0001A6B6) | | | |
