Beitild, owner of Iron-Breaker Mine

**Beitild** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [miner](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner_(class) "Skyrim:Miner (class)") who owns [Iron-Breaker Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron-Breaker_Mine "Skyrim:Iron-Breaker Mine") in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). She is married to [Leigelf](/wiki/Skyrim:Leigelf "Skyrim:Leigelf"), owner of [Quicksilver Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Mine "Skyrim:Quicksilver Mine"), though their feud has caused them to live in separate houses. She will [pay for](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") any [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") you dig up, and doing so will increase her [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") towards you. Beitild is also a target of a [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") [contract](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Beitild "Skyrim:Kill Beitild").

She gets up at 6am for a one-hour breakfast, then heads to work in Iron-Breaker Mine, pausing at noon and 7pm for a one-hour lunch. She ends her workday at midnight and goes [home](/wiki/Skyrim:Beitild%27s_House "Skyrim:Beitild's House") for sleep.

She wears a set of [miner's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner%27s_Clothes "Skyrim:Miner's Clothes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#00080699 "Skyrim:Boots"), and is equipped with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"). She carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Beitild%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Beitild's House") to [her house](/wiki/Skyrim:Beitild%27s_House "Skyrim:Beitild's House") and a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Kill Beitild](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Beitild "Skyrim:Kill Beitild")**: Resolve a feud in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").
- **[Mine Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore")**: Get paid to [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") ore. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Kill Beitild

Like with most targets of the Dark Brotherhood, you may also have a word with Beitild before killing her. She will not be welcoming:

:   *"I'm really not in the mood. State your business, or take your leave."*

If you walk away instead of answering her, approaching her again will have her tell you:

:   *"I'm busy, and you're bothering me. So go away."*

You have an option of three replies:

| Topic | Dialogue | Response |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Someone wants you dead, Beitild.** | *"And let me guess, that someone is my so-called husband Leigelf? Well the feeling's mutual."* | Walks away |
| **I represent the Dark Brotherhood. Your death is at hand!** | *"What? Well, we'll see about that now, won't we?"* | Draws her pickaxe and attacks |
| **(Remain Silent)** | *"I've a mine to run, so if you'll excuse me..."* | Walks away |

## Dialogue

When approached she can potentially say:

:   *"Iron-Breaker Mine is three times the worth of that Quicksilver Mine and its fat-head owner."*
:   *"My miners are as dumb as rocks are grey."*
:   *"Mining is hard work, but we pay a fair price for any ore you dig up."*

Should Leigelf die, she may remark about it when approached:

:   *"My husband Leigelf is dead. I... I never thought I would miss that oaf so much."*

When spoken to directly:

:   **Who's in charge around here?**
:   *"That would be Jarl [Skald the Elder](/wiki/Skyrim:Skald "Skyrim:Skald"). He's over in [the White Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Hall "Skyrim:The White Hall"), probably talking about [Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") like he's the second coming of [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos")."*

:   *"Jarl [Brina Merilis](/wiki/Skyrim:Brina_Merilis "Skyrim:Brina Merilis") is in charge, thanks to the Empire. Best hide any Talos amulets you have."* **(If Dawnstar is taken by the Imperial Legion)**

:   **What do you do in Dawnstar?**
:   *"I own Iron-Breaker Mine. We make twice as much coin as those horkers over in Quicksilver Mine, and don't let anyone tell you otherwise.
    I pay a good wage for any iron ore you dig up, if you're looking for work."*

If [Waking Nightmare](/wiki/Skyrim:Waking_Nightmare "Skyrim:Waking Nightmare") has not been completed and Dawnstar is still plagued by nightmares, she may tell you:

:   *"You're wrong to come here, stranger. No rest in Dawnstar."*
:   **"No rest in Dawnstar"?**
:   *"Everyone here is having nightmares. I have miners tripping over their own feet from lack of sleep. I heard there was a [Priest of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Erandur "Skyrim:Erandur") who was supposed to be looking into it. We'll see if anything comes of that."*

### Conversations

If Leigelf is still alive, Beitild may tell [Karl](/wiki/Skyrim:Karl "Skyrim:Karl"), one of her workers, about her feud with Leigelf:

:   **Beitild:** *"Keep at it. We need to work twice as hard now that fat-headed Leigelf has declared war!"*
:   **Karl:** *"We're at war with Leigelf? Isn't he your husband?"*
:   **Beitild:** *"No he isn't! He's the enemy, and we are going to crush him."*
:   **Karl:** *"Drafted into a war, how could my life get worse?"*

She can also be found urging Karl to work harder:

:   **Beitild:** *"Work hard, now! The pride of Iron-Breaker Mine is on the line."*
:   **Karl:** *"Pride of the what? This isn't the Legion, boss. We're miners, not soldiers."*
:   **Beitild:** *"You'll shut your mouth and get back to work, or you won't be a miner or a soldier by the day's end. Hear me?"*
:   **Karl:** *"Uh, yes ma'am."*

## Unused Dialogue

Beitild has unused dialogue tied to the [unfinished quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfinished_Quests "Skyrim:Unfinished Quests") `FreeformDawnstarA` she was once meant to play a role in. This dialogue can only be found in the game's DialogueViews files, and not the Creation Kit.

It seems that this quest could be started by talking to either Beitild or Leigelf, and both would talk about their feud. Beitild would say:

:   **Are you and your husband fighting?**
:   *"He doesn't respect me. Always going on about he could run the mine better without my help. Well, I'm going to show him. Let's see him say he doesn't need me when he's out of business."*

You would then discover a journal belonging to Leigelf inside of his house. The journal would confirm that he actually still loves his wife. You could then bring the journal to either Beitild or Leigelf:

:   **You might be interested in this journal I found.**
:   *"A journal? What do I care about some journal? I have a mine to run."*

:   :   **It's your *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* husband, Leigelf. He says he still loves you.**
    :   *"Let me see that... Oh, Leigelf, you big oaf. You felt this way the whole time? I need to talk to my husband. Thank you for bringing this to me."*

It can be assumed that by the end of this quest, the feud between the two would be resolved, but the consequences for the mines or its employees are unknown.

## Notes

- The *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* refers to her as **Beitild Iron-Breaker**, implying the mine bears her clan name, rather than being named after the type of ore found inside.
- Once you've received your orders to kill Beitild, you may ask [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") about her. He will say, *"She separated from her husband several months ago. Now the two run competing mining operations. Beitild's angry and desperate. A fighter."*
- Should Beitild die, either by your hand or otherwise, then approaching Leigelf may have him tell you, *"My wife Beitild is dead. Can't say I miss that old sabre cat."*

Belchimac

**Belchimac** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [miner](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner_(class) "Skyrim:Miner (class)") who lives and works in [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten").

He sleeps in [Karthwasten Miner's Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten_Miner%27s_Barracks "Skyrim:Karthwasten Miner's Barracks") from midnight to 8am, and works in [Sanuarach Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanuarach_Mine "Skyrim:Sanuarach Mine") between 8am and 8pm. He spends the rest of the evening relaxing in the barracks.

He wears a set of [miner's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner%27s_Clothes#00080697 "Skyrim:Miner's Clothes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#00080699 "Skyrim:Clothing"), and is equipped with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"). He carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Karthwasten_Miners%27_Barracks "Skyrim:Key to Karthwasten Miners' Barracks") to the miner's barracks and a selection of [lower-class loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Sanuarach Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanuarach_Mine_(quest) "Skyrim:Sanuarach Mine (quest)")**: End the dispute over [Sanuarach Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanuarach_Mine "Skyrim:Sanuarach Mine").
- **[The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella")**: Find a new [Sybil](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra") for the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella").

### The Heart of Dibella

When asked if he knows where a [young girl](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra") who lives here is:

:   **I'm looking for a young girl who lives around here.**
:   *"Yeah, we're all looking for something."*

## Dialogue

Before you reopen the mines, he'll be depressed, saying:

:   *"The good mine is closed and the [other mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Fenn%27s_Gulch_Mine "Skyrim:Fenn's Gulch Mine") has no ore. Gods have cursed me."*

He'll keep his attitude when they're open:

:   *"Sauranach*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *mine is open again. How am I supposed to handle all this work?"*

## Conversations

He can often be seen talking to other miners:

:   **[Enmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Enmon "Skyrim:Enmon")**: *"When are those [Silver-Blood men](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Mercenary "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Mercenary") going to leave?"*
:   **Belchimac**: *"Never. They've shut us down forever, Enmon. The Divines have abandoned us."*

:   **Belchimac**: *"We're doomed. The mine is going to stay closed, and we'll up*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *be carted of*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *to [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine") as slaves."*
:   **Enmon**: *"Only criminals get sent to Cidhna Mine. They're not going to send us there."*
:   **Belchimac**: *"Oh, they'll find some way to send us there. It'll be just my luck."*

:   **Belchimac**: *"Damn [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord"). Always getting in the way of us honest folk."*
:   **[Ragnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragnar "Skyrim:Ragnar")**: *"What did you say? You lazy coward, I'll cut your throat."*
:   **Belchimac**: *"Nothing, Ragnar. Please... don't hurt me."*
:   **Ragnar**: *"I... I'm sorry, Belchimac. I didn't mean that."*

:   **Ragnar**: *"You're always talking about the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). You aren't thinking of joining them, are you?"*
:   **Belchimac**: *"Maybe I will. What do you think about that?"*
:   **Ragnar**: *"I'm warning you. Those people are killers. You'd never last a day with them."*

:   **Belchimac**: *"I don't like bunking with [Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc"). It's not... clean."*
:   **[Lash](/wiki/Skyrim:Lash_gra-Dushnikh "Skyrim:Lash gra-Dushnikh")**: *"If you want me to leave, you could challenge me to a fight. I promise to stop once you've lost an arm."*
:   **Belchimac**: *"What I meant to say was... I love having an Orc here in the barracks. They're so... pleasant."*

:   **Lash**: *"Why do your people claim the [Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") is theirs? The Orcs have been in these lands just as long."*
:   **Belchimac**: *"You wouldn't understand, Lash. Your people aren't smart enough for politics."*
:   **Lash**: *"Is that so? I'll remember that next time we're in the mine tunnels... alone."*
:   **Belchimac**: *"Did... did I say you weren't smart? I meant to say that I'm not smart, Lash. I'm just not smart enough to answer your questions."*

## Bugs

- Belchimac does not have a cleanup script attached, which may result in his corpse persisting indefinitely.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.

Beldama Witch

**Beldama Witches** are hostile witches who guard [Beldama Ward Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Beldama_Ward_Mother "Skyrim:Beldama Ward Mother"), appear at [Karthspire Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthspire_Camp "Skyrim:Karthspire Camp") during [Crypt of the Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Crypt_of_the_Heart "Skyrim:Crypt of the Heart"), in front of the rock where the dead [Daenella](/wiki/Skyrim:Daenella "Skyrim:Daenella") lies.

They wear [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes") with matching [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"). One of them carries *[Beldama Witch's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Beldama_Witch%27s_Note "Skyrim:Beldama Witch's Note")*. Their appearance may differ more than two types shown in the picture.

## Overview

Belethor's General Goods

**Belethor's General Goods** is a store in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")'s market area of the Plains District. It is located next door to [Arcadia's Cauldron](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia%27s_Cauldron "Skyrim:Arcadia's Cauldron"), opposite [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare").

As a general goods merchant, [Belethor](/wiki/Skyrim:Belethor "Skyrim:Belethor") buys and sells any type of item. His assistant [Sigurd](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigurd "Skyrim:Sigurd") helps out around the shop and is often outside chopping wood at the [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") on the northwest side. The shop is open during normal business hours, from 8am to 8pm. It contains only one zone, the [interior](#Belethor.27s_General_Goods).

**NOTE**: Like all other stores, Belethor's General Goods has a number of fixed wares on display scattered around the main trading room. These can be bought from the proprietor, Belethor, and will disappear from the room when purchased. For a list of these special items, see [this section](#Displayed_Merchandise).

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Belethor](/wiki/Skyrim:Belethor "Skyrim:Belethor") [General Goods](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "General Goods")  [Sigurd](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigurd "Skyrim:Sigurd") |

## Belethor's General Goods

Inside Belethor's General Goods

Entry is into the main store, with a large firepit against the southeast wall, which has an empty pot hanging over it. The counter comes out from the northwest wall and extends about halfway across the room. The counter is filled with [displayed merchandise](#Displayed_Merchandise) that can either be bought or stolen, while under the counter is a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl"). There is a low table in front of the counter and a dresser with a couple of display racks full of displayed merchandise on top against the northeast wall. On the northwest wall there is a row of three wall shelves coming down the wall in the row, with a chair and small dresser further to the left. There are two doors out of this room; one in the eastern corner and one in the southern corner. There is also a doorway behind the counter in the middle of the southwest wall. To the right of the door in the southern corner is a cupboard with a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Biography of the Wolf Queen](/wiki/Skyrim:Biography_of_the_Wolf_Queen "Skyrim:Biography of the Wolf Queen")*. Behind the counter against the southwest wall, to the right of the door, are two sets of shelves holding displayed merchandise. In addition to the displayed merchandise around the room there are several bowls, [plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate"), [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"), a [candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlestick "Skyrim:Candlestick"), and many [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks.

The doorway leads to a back room that has the second entrance in the eastern corner, with a firepit in the southern corner which has an empty pot hanging over it as well as two bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and two [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") hanging from the ceiling above. Beside the firepit, against the southwest wall, is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand, while in the western corner there is a small square wooden table and two chairs. On the table is an [Eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel") and a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") on a plate with a goblet. Above the table on the northwest wall are two wall shelves holding various plates, [cups](/wiki/Skyrim:Cup "Skyrim:Cup") and a bowl containing a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd").

The door in the southern corner leads to a collection of crates and barrels under the stairs leading up to the top floor that is accessed through the other door in the eastern corner. Climbing the stairs leads to the living quarters with only a third of the floor being slatted in an L-shape, with a door on the left that leads to [Belethor](/wiki/Skyrim:Belethor "Skyrim:Belethor")'s bedroom. In the front is a dresser with the [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger") on top. To the right along the northwest wall is a low table and chairs. On the table is an apprentice-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") containing random items, a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bowl, a plate, and [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") on top. In the northern corner is [Sigurd](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigurd "Skyrim:Sigurd")'s single owned bed. Belethor's bedroom consists of his large double bed in the middle of the northwest wall with an end table on either side and a set of shelves holding nothing of interest against the northeast wall beside the door.

## Displayed Merchandise

The following items are sitting out in the store, for example on the store counters. They can be purchased from the merchant, or else can be stolen. Other items may also be present in the store, but those other items are not available for purchase. They [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") after ten days.

|  |
| --- |
| - **Food**: 1 [Goat Cheese Wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), 2 [Leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), 3 [Potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), 6 [Red Apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), 1 [Sliced Eidar Cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), 5 [Tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato") - **Books**: 1 *[Beggar Prince](/wiki/Lore:Beggar_Prince "Lore:Beggar Prince")*, 1 *[Biography of Barenziah v1, v2, v3](/wiki/Lore:Biography_of_Barenziah "Lore:Biography of Barenziah")*, 1 *[Fall from Glory](/wiki/Lore:Fall_from_Glory "Lore:Fall from Glory")*, 1 *[Nightingales: Fact or Fiction?](/wiki/Lore:Nightingales:_Fact_or_Fiction%3F "Lore:Nightingales: Fact or Fiction?")*, 1 *[Uncommon Taste](/wiki/Lore:Uncommon_Taste "Lore:Uncommon Taste")* - **Misc**: 1 [Candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlestick "Skyrim:Candlestick"), 1 [Cave Bear Pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Cave_Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Cave Bear Pelt"), 1 [Goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"), 1 [Horker Tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk"), 2 [Jugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug"), 1 [Pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Pot "Skyrim:Pot"), 1 [Tankard](/wiki/Skyrim:Tankard "Skyrim:Tankard"), 1 [Troll Skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull") |

## Notes

- There is a "Loot" [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") to the right of the entrance door.
- The game has a preference for the rear door on the southeast side; even if you enter via the door from the market, your follower will enter using the other door, and all quest targets outside the shop will point to the rear door.
- All containers in the area are non-respawning and safe to store items in if you wish, with the exception of some barrels and sacks.
- Investing here also adds gold to [Khajiit caravans](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders").

## Bugs

- The potato on the floor behind the counter may be wedged into the wall, with no way to retrieve it. **?**
- Joining the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") may allow you to take some of the items in the front of the store for free without it being considered theft. **?**

# Skyrim:Belethor

## Overview

| Belethor (RefID: 0001A672) | | | |

Belethor

**Belethor** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [pawnbroker](/wiki/Skyrim:Pawnbroker "Skyrim:Pawnbroker") and also the owner of [Belethor's General Goods](/wiki/Skyrim:Belethor%27s_General_Goods "Skyrim:Belethor's General Goods") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). As a general merchant, he buys and sells almost everything.

Belethor lives the life of a busy merchant and therefore spends much of his time running his store. He wakes up at 8am and immediately opens up the shop for business. He can be found behind the counter inside the shop for the next twelve hours, offering his services to any potential customers. At 8pm, he leaves his shop to begin a four-hour stroll around Whiterun. From his shop, he heads west toward the main gate to Whiterun. Once he reaches the intersection before the [Guard Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Barracks_(Gate) "Skyrim:Guard Barracks (Gate)") by the gate, he turns right and heads north up the steps to reach the Wind District. He will walk past [Amren's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren%27s_House "Skyrim:Amren's House") and [House Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:House_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:House Gray-Mane") to eventually reach the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen"). At this point, he will head down the steps to the south to reach the market stalls in the Plains District and he will eventually reach the starting point of his stroll around Whiterun, his store. He will repeat this route until midnight, when he returns to his store, heads upstairs to his bed, and sleeps for the next eight hours.

Belethor wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000261c0 "Skyrim:Clothing"), a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000261bd "Skyrim:Clothing"), and a pair of [gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000261c1 "Skyrim:Clothing"). He is equipped with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Belethor%27s_General_Goods "Skyrim:Key to Belethor's General Goods") to his store, as well as a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

His greetings can be:

:   *"Everything's for sale my friend. Everything. If I had a sister I'd sell her in a second."*
:   *"I'd even buy one of your relatives, if you're looking to sell. Ha ha ha ha. That's a little joke."*
:   *"You just let me know what you need. I am at your beck and call."*
:   *"Imperials, Stormcloaks... I don't care who's in charge around here. I just want to make money!"*
:   *"Welcome to Belethor's General Goods. Welcome, indeed."*
:   *"I know what you're thinking: "This Belethor, how could he part with such magnificent treasures?""*
:   *"I can tell you're a discriminating customer. Perhaps you're a wealthy one, too, hm?"*
:   *"Everything's for sale, my friend! You need visit no other shops today!"*
:   *"I assure you, I'm prepared to make any deal."*
:   *"Please, do look around. I'm sure I have something you'll want."*

When spoken to directly he can be asked questions about himself and his business:

:   **What brings a Breton to Skyrim?**
:   *"Isn't it obvious? Why, the wonderful weather and hospitable people, of course! Not to mention my great fondness for [dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") and petty political [power struggles](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"). Ah, but without a doubt, the most compelling feature of this frozen wasteland is the volley of inane questions leveled at me on a regular basis."*

:   **How's business?**
:   *"Interesting, to say the least. What with all that's been going on. On the one hand, supplies are harder to come by, since fewer traders are traveling the roads these days. But on the other, the scarcity of supplies has led to some, well, 'elevated' prices. All that matters is that I have what you need. And it's worth every septim."*

After the [siege on Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)"), you may ask him about his business again. Belethor will again reply with sarcasm:

:   **The siege must have been hard on the city's merchants.**
:   *"Oh no, not at all. I simply locked the doors, hid beneath my counter and prayed to the Divines that my life would be spared and my shop wouldn't burn to the ground. But other than that, everything was business as usual. Now, do you have any other painfully obvious things to say?"*

If you choose to invest in his shop:

:   **I'd like to make an investment in your business.**
:   *"I'll take your money, but I make no promises of a large return on your investment. These are troubled times, after all."*
:   **Let's see what you can do with this.**
:   *"Ah, the sound of clinking coins. Even better, the sound of clinking coins in my hand!"*

When exiting conversation he may say:

:   *"Do come back."*
:   *"Remember, I'll give you the best deals, or die trying."*
:   *"Next time, come see my*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *at my shop. I've got some things you'll just love."*

## Notes

- Belethor is mistakenly referred to as a [Wood Elf](/wiki/Lore:Wood_Elf "Lore:Wood Elf") by the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")*.

## Bugs

- Occasionally, Belethor will display a blank inventory with neither the option to buy or sell. It is not known what causes this and the bug is permanent once it occurs.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.
- Belethor's shop will often close the moment you leave no matter what the hour, and may not reopen until after his inventory resets. This can be particularly annoying if you buy a high gold item intending to return with goods to trade the same day. Similarly, you may not be able to return to acquire an item seen before the reset occurs if you leave to get goods to trade. The standard wait for reset often results in his shop still being closed regardless of the time of day.

  **Mod Notes**: His active package is targeting `000cab88`, but even if moved and allowed to walk back again, he'll never make it there.

  - Waiting nearby in one-hour increments may fix this.
  - Belethor may continue to sell items normally if you pick the lock during business hours.
  -  Enter the console command `prid 1a672` followed by `disable` and then `enable`. This may take a few seconds to take effect.
  - One way this can happen is if Belethor is speaking while you exit the building, causing him to follow you outside. To avoid this, make sure he finishes any idle dialogue before activating the door.
- [Ysolda](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda "Skyrim:Ysolda") was intended to take over Belethor's duties if he was killed, but she does not correctly do so, making her unable to be traded with.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.

Beleval

**Beleval** is a [Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") and a member of the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"), who can be found in [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard"). Like most other recruits, she is available as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"), and with [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") installed, she is available as your [personal steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward "Skyrim:Personal Steward").

She arrives at Fort Dawnguard when you reach [stage 60](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard)#Quest_Stages "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)") of the quest [Prophet](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)"). She will then join the growing team of recruits hanging out in the western area and will spend her time wandering, relaxing, eating or using the various tools in the area. On every full hour, she may decide to train her [crossbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Crossbow "Skyrim:Crossbow") skills on the dummies in the northern cave for three hours. She sleeps on one of the cots between 8pm and 4am. During the [Kindred Judgment](/wiki/Skyrim:Kindred_Judgment "Skyrim:Kindred Judgment") quest, she will be in the crowd when [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran") holds his [speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran#Kindred_Judgement "Skyrim:Isran"), although she will not participate in the attack on [Volkihar Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep").

She is clad in a set of Dawnguard heavy equipment. This includes the brown [cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Dawnguard Heavy Armor"), as well as matching pairs of [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Heavy_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Dawnguard Heavy Gauntlets") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Heavy_Boots "Skyrim:Dawnguard Heavy Boots"). She is equipped with a [Dawnguard war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_War_Axe "Skyrim:Dawnguard War Axe") and a [crossbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Crossbow "Skyrim:Crossbow") supplemented with fifteen [steel bolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Bolt "Skyrim:Steel Bolt").

## Related Quests

- **[Destroying the Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroying_the_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Destroying the Dawnguard")**: Kill the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)") leaders.
- **[Kindred Judgment](/wiki/Skyrim:Kindred_Judgment "Skyrim:Kindred Judgment")**: Confront [Lord Harkon](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Harkon "Skyrim:Lord Harkon").

## Dialogue

If you are an elf, she will say:

:   *"Not a lot of our kind here, I see. Suppose I shouldn't be surprised. Still, those of us here have as much of an obligation to protect Skyrim as any other, wouldn't you agree?"*

If you are not an elf, she will instead say:

:   *"Seems that I'm the only of my kind here. Suppose I shouldn't be surprised. Still, it's my duty to help protect Skyrim as much as any Nord's, don't you think?"*

You can also ask her why she joined the Dawnguard:

:   **Why did you join the Dawnguard?**
:   *"[Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran") is the only one trying to do something about these vampires. I don't much like him, but I can't allow the people of Skyrim to be preyed upon by those monsters."*

## Notes

-  The Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch 3.0.1 changes it so that Beleval participates in the attack on Castle Volkihar.
- Beleval is the only female Bosmer [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") in the game.
- Although her default gear is governed by the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") skill, Beleval is actually more proficient in [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor").

## Bugs

- Due to Beleval using the `FemaleSultry` voicetype, and said voicetype not generally being supported for follower dialogue, many of her follower lines will be completely silent, as they have no corresponding voice file attached.
  - This problem is shared by [Eola](/wiki/Skyrim:Eola "Skyrim:Eola"), another follower making use of this particular voicetype.
- Beleval may not regenerate after entering bleedout because she inherited stats from the bandit templates where the bleedout override checkbox was enabled.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.0.8, fixes this bug.

Belrand

**Belrand** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [spellsword](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCclassBelrand "Skyrim:NPCclassBelrand") and [blade-for-hire](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") who can be found in the [Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). He charges a fee of 500 gold.

He wears a set of [iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor"), a pair of [hide bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers"), and a pair of [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots"). He is equipped with an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"). He knows the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") spell [Oakflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Oakflesh "Skyrim:Oakflesh"), the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") spell [Conjure Familiar](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Familiar "Skyrim:Conjure Familiar"), and the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") spells [Fast Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fast_Healing "Skyrim:Fast Healing") and [Lesser Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Ward "Skyrim:Lesser Ward").

Belrand can join the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades"), and can also be a potential [marriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") partner.

## Related Quests

- **[The Bonds of Matrimony](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bonds_of_Matrimony "Skyrim:The Bonds of Matrimony")**: Find someone in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") to [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").
- **[Rebuilding the Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades")**: Recruit new members for the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades").

## Dialogue

He will glowingly advertise his services with:

:   *"Versatility is the key to survival. Hire me, and you'll be well prepared to face threats both magical and mundane."*
:   *"I fight with both blade and spell. You might say I'm equipped to handle nearly any threat. So, shall we talk price?"*
:   *"Sure, you can hire a swordsman or a spellcaster to fight at your side, but why not get both for the price of one?"*
:   *"By blade or by spell, if you want it dead, I'll make it dead. All you need to do is pay my fee."*
:   *"The blade can be as lethal as the spell, but deadlier still is the one who wields both!"*

If you heed his endorsement and hire him, he will gleefully say, *"What dangers and wonders shall we discover in the frozen wastes? I can hardly wait to find out!"*

After being hired, Belrand will occasionally greet you with, *"You're looking hale and healthy. It's good to see you again."* or "*Didn't think I'd be seeing you again so soon."* Like other hirelings, he may offer his services free of charge after being dismissed, saying, *"Back for more? Since we had so much fun the last time, I'll join you free of charge."* If you accept, he will tell you, *"Lead the way."*

## Follower Dialogue

| Your Line | Belrand's Response |
| --- | --- |
| **Follow me.** | *"Onward to our next adventure!"* |
| **Wait here.** | *"Very well. Just be careful!"* |
| **I need you to do something.** | *"All right. What is it?"* |
| **I need to trade some things with you.** | *"Do I get to keep it? Nah... Just kidding."* |
| **It's time for us to part ways.** | *"If that's what you want. Watch your back out there, and if you need me again, you know where I'll be."* |

## Notes

- He wears a heavy cuirass, despite being proficient in light armor instead. In addition, despite having a high [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") skill and a perk for Destruction, he knows no Destruction spells.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.8, addresses this issue. He is now fully clad in hide armor, and has the ability to cast [Ice Spike](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Spike "Skyrim:Ice Spike").
- In the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit") data, there's an outfit named `BelrandOutfit`, which consists of a leveled piece of light armor boots, cuirass, and gauntlets of the best quality. However, it isn't in use.

## Bugs

- He exhibits the [mercenary followers bug](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward#Bugs "Skyrim:Personal Steward") as a [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward "Skyrim:Personal Steward")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire").
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.

Belyn Hlaalu's House

**Belyn Hlaalu's House** is a small home in the Gray Quarter of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). It is the first house on the left when entering the Quarter from [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall").

It is the home of [Belyn Hlaalu](/wiki/Skyrim:Belyn_Hlaalu "Skyrim:Belyn Hlaalu"), the owner of [Hlaalu Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Hlaalu_Farm "Skyrim:Hlaalu Farm"), who lives here alone. It consists of one area, *[Belyn Hlaalu's House](#Belyn_Hlaalu.27s_House)*.

## Residents

| Name |
| --- |
| [Belyn Hlaalu](/wiki/Skyrim:Belyn_Hlaalu "Skyrim:Belyn Hlaalu") |

## Belyn Hlaalu's House

Inside Belyn Hlaalu's House

The front door opens to the sight of an old cart stashed underneath a ladder leading upstairs. Along the eastern wall sits an end table containing clutter, with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") on top. At the foot of the ladder is a dresser with [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing "Skyrim:Clothing"). An entrance to the west leads to the dining area; the southeastern corner has seven food sacks, while the nearby set of shelves holds a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a [honey nut treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat"), three heads of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), a sample of [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota"), a bouquet of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), and a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). Leaning against the shelves is another pickaxe. The obligatory fireplace can be found along the southern wall, with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") above the hot embers, and a head of [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") leaning against the wall. The table in the southwestern corner holds three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a wedge of [goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), and a wedge of [Eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"). The dinner table only seats one, and has more food, including a slice of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [boiled creme treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), some [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), and a bottle of regular [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). Lastly, the shelves in the northeastern corner have two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of regular wine, and a Nord mead on display.

The upstairs area is spacious, but also rather bare. At the top of the stairs is a small table with a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). In the bedroom, two food barrels decorate the southeastern corner, one of them located right next to Belyn's owned bed. In the adjacent corner is an end table with clutter, a copy of *[Dunmer of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmer_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Dunmer of Skyrim")*, and a respawning [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Knapsack "Skyrim:Containers") with leveled items. The chest contains random items, while the dresser contains random [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing "Skyrim:Clothing"). More clothes are scattered around the dresser: a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#Boots "Skyrim:Clothing"), a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#Hats "Skyrim:Clothing"), and a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"). Hidden behind the dresser is a copy of the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Frostfall, v10](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Frostfall,_v10 "Skyrim:2920, Frostfall, v10")*.

## Notes

- With the exception of some barrels, sacks, and the knapsack, all containers in the area are non-respawning and safe to store items in.

## Overview

Belyn Hlaalu at his farm

**Belyn Hlaalu** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") living in his [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Belyn_Hlaalu%27s_House "Skyrim:Belyn Hlaalu's House") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). He is also the owner of [Hlaalu Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Hlaalu_Farm "Skyrim:Hlaalu Farm"), a small [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") farm just outside the city walls that he runs with his employee, [Adisla](/wiki/Skyrim:Adisla "Skyrim:Adisla"). He will [pay you](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat") 5 gold for any wheat you might have harvested.

Belyn wakes up at 7am and stays in his house for three hours to enjoy his breakfast. At 10am he heads down to the Hlaalu Farm to oversee its functioning and help Adisla get some work done. At 6pm Belyn leaves the farm and visits the [New Gnisis Cornerclub](/wiki/Skyrim:New_Gnisis_Cornerclub "Skyrim:New Gnisis Cornerclub") where he eats his dinner until 10pm when he heads home to his bed.

His outfit consists of a set of [miner's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner%27s_Clothes#00080697 "Skyrim:Miner's Clothes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#00080699 "Skyrim:Boots"). Belyn carries around the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Belyn_Hlaalu%27s_House_Key "Skyrim:Belyn Hlaalu's House Key") to his house, along with a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: Get paid to gather crops. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This NPC is one of many potential quest givers or quest targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_NPCs "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Dialogue

He is very proud of his farm and gladly shares his philosophy:

:   *"The best way for us to win the Nords' respect is through hard work."*
:   *"Too many dark elves in Windhelm complain about the way we're treated. What good does complaining do?"*
:   *"I'm proud of my farm. It takes no small effort to grow crops in this part of Skyrim."*

## Conversations

Belyn and Adisla

Belyn will hold a number of conversations with his employee Adisla. One will have Adisla ask him about a wheat shipment:

:   **Adisla**: *"I was wondering if you had ordered the shipment of that frostwheat, sir."*
:   **Belyn**: *"Yes, but that fool [Endario](/wiki/Skyrim:Orthus_Endario "Skyrim:Orthus Endario") can't get it in. I'll thrash him when I get back to the city, don't you worry."*
:   **Adisla**: *"I wasn't wanting to get anyone in trouble, sir. Just wanting to get the new planting started, is all."*
:   **Belyn**: *"Yes, wouldn't want to miss the lush summer we have ahead."*

In another conversation between the two, Belyn will order Adisla to perform repairs around the farm, and criticize her resource usage:

:   **Belyn**: *"Make sure the back fence is repaired. I swear I saw some [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") in nibbling the leaves yesterday. "*
:   **Adisla**: *"Oh, no skeevers out here, sir. They can't stand the cold."*
:   **Belyn**: *"Maybe, but the way you burn through all that wood to keep the cabin toasty, they might mistake this place for [Elsweyr](/wiki/Lore:Elsweyr "Lore:Elsweyr")."*
:   **Adisla**: *"Sorry, sir. These old bones do like a bit of warmth in the evening. There's no need to make fun."*
:   **Belyn**: *"You just need to remember that there's a war on, and firewood isn't cheap these days."*

In another, Belyn will ask her about [Captain Lonely-Gale](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Lonely-Gale "Skyrim:Captain Lonely-Gale"):

:   **Belyn**: *"So have you ever actually spoken to Captain Lonely-Gale?"*
:   **Adisla**: *"By the gods, he's just a retired ship's captain."*
:   **Belyn**: *"Maybe to you, but he's just so... his story is..."*
:   **Adisla**: *"He's just a guard captain. And not a very good one, at that."*

Adisla will also make mention of her age impeding her ability to work the farm: *"Starting to get too old to work all day, but hopefully Master Hlaalu will let me slow down a bit."*

## Notes

- According to *[Dunmer of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmer_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Dunmer of Skyrim")*, he is a descendant of the Dunmer [House Hlaalu](/wiki/Lore:House_Hlaalu "Lore:House Hlaalu").
- He shares a surname with [Niluva Hlaalu](/wiki/Skyrim:Niluva_Hlaalu "Skyrim:Niluva Hlaalu") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). While her dialogue implies that Niluva is also a descendant of the former Great House, there is nothing to suggest they know of each other, or are related in any way.

Bendt

**Bendt** is an [elderly](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder "Skyrim:Elder") cook working the kitchen in the basement of the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College"). He is not particularly fond of people entering his premises, which might explain why the majority of students enjoy their meals at the local tavern instead.

He lives a secluded life in the kitchen area of the college. Like the students, he wakes up early at 4am then spends the entire day in the kitchen, where he either cooks, eats, or wanders around. At 10pm he enters his private quarters and goes to bed. The only exception to this routine occurs at the end of [Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames") when he will set up a small stand in the courtyard outside the college, celebrating the annual Burning of King Olaf festival.

He wears a [chef's tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Chef%27s_Tunic "Skyrim:Chef's Tunic") with a matching [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Chef%27s_Hat "Skyrim:Chef's Hat") and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#00018801 "Skyrim:Clothing"). He only carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Evette_San%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Evette San's House") to [Evette San](/wiki/Skyrim:Evette_San "Skyrim:Evette San")'s house (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

## Dialogue

When approached in his kitchen, he makes it quite clear that you are not welcome, saying:

:   *"You've found the Bards College kitchen. Congratulations."*
:   *"Meals are served to Bards at designated times. Find an inn if you want to make requests."*
:   *"You look a little sturdier than most of the Popinjays around here."*

During the Festival, he will be a bit more polite, shouting:

:   *"Candy! Get your King Olaf's Festival candy!"*
:   *"Tasty, sugary treats!"*

If you approach him, he will offer you his treats with:

:   *"You might as well have some sweets. I made them for the festival after all."*

## Related Quests

- **[Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames")**: Unveil the truth about a deceitful [King](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_One-Eye "Skyrim:Olaf One-Eye") and become a member of the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College").

## Bugs

- Bendt was mistakenly given the key to Evette San's house, despite having no relations with her at all.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=8512))

# Skyrim:Beneath Bronze Waters

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Investigate the waters outside [Bronze Water Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bronze_Water_Cave "Skyrim:Bronze Water Cave").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Viriya](/wiki/Skyrim:Viriya "Skyrim:Viriya") |
| Location(s): | [Bronze Water Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bronze_Water_Cave "Skyrim:Bronze Water Cave"), [Alftand Ruined Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand_Ruined_Tower "Skyrim:Alftand Ruined Tower"), [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") |
| Reward: | [Dwarven Fishing Rod](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Fishing_Rod "Skyrim:Dwarven Fishing Rod"), [Irkngthand War Axe of Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Irkngthand_War_Axe_of_Fire "Skyrim:Irkngthand War Axe of Fire"), [Irkngthand War Axe of Freezing](/wiki/Skyrim:Irkngthand_War_Axe_of_Freezing "Skyrim:Irkngthand War Axe of Freezing") |

Beneath Bronze Waters

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to Bronze Water Cave.
2. Read the fisherman's journal.
3. Find the Dwarven fishing rod schematic in Alftand Ruined Tower.
4. Bring the Dwarven fishing rod schematic to Calcelmo.
5. Use the dwarven fishing rod to catch two aetherium dynamo cores near Bronze Water Cave.
6. Insert the aetherium dynamo cores into the dynamo actuators.

## Detailed Walkthrough

The schematics

This quest can be started after [The Ultimate Feast](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ultimate_Feast "Skyrim:The Ultimate Feast") has been completed by talking to Viriya:

:   **Know of anyone in need of fishing work around Skyrim?**
:   *"Of course. It's all in this note."*

She will then hand you a [bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Dwarven_Investigation "Skyrim:Bounty: Dwarven Investigation") that asks you to investigate the outside of Bronze Water Cave. As you arrive at the cave, you will have to pick up and read the [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Fisherman%27s_Journal_(Fishing) "Skyrim:Fisherman's Journal (Fishing)") that is on a plank of wood. The journal mentions a fishing rod of Dwarven make that might be found in [Alftand Ruined Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand_Ruined_Tower "Skyrim:Alftand Ruined Tower").

Travel to Alftand Ruined Tower and after a short while inside you will find the dead body of [Jorid](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorid "Skyrim:Jorid"), the fisherman mentioned in the journal. Press the button on the desk near the body, but be careful as it will activate flamethrowers ahead of you while opening the door.

Head through the now open door, but be wary of the pressure plates on the floor as they will activate spears. You will find the [Dwarven Fishing Rod Schematic](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Items#Miscellaneous_Items "Skyrim:Fishing Items") on a desk. Once obtained you will need to take the schematics to Calcelmo and speak to him:

:   **I investigated Bronze Water Cave and discovered a dormant Dwarven mechanism.**
:   *"Yes..."*
:   **Fishermen saw glowing objects that may activate it, but couldn't retrieve them.**
:   *"Hmmm... No, that's probably not of any use."*
:   **They believed using a Dwarven fishing rod might help. Here are the schematics.**
:   *"Ah, yes! There it is! Thank you so much."*
:   **In exchange for the schematic, could you build a Dwarven fishing rod for me?**
:   *"Of course."*

You will then need to wait 24 hours and return to Calcelmo:

:   **I've returned. Is the Dwarven fishing rod complete?**
:   *"I've been holding onto this for you. Here! I hope you like it."*
:   **Consider the bounty paid in full. I'll try using this near Bronze Water Cave.**
:   *"Oh, now, do be careful..."*

At this point you will not only acquire a [Dwarven Fishing Rod](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Fishing_Rod "Skyrim:Dwarven Fishing Rod") but unlock the ability to create Dwarven Fishing Rods yourself, just in case you misplace the first one.

The chest rises.

Head back to Bronze Water Cave where you will have to fish in two spots for the [Aetherium Dynamo Cores](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Items#Miscellaneous_Items "Skyrim:Fishing Items"). Once you have fished them up, place them into the dynamo actuators. This will cause a chest to rise from the water, but will also activate some dwarven spider workers by the cave entrance. Once the dwarven spider workers have been dealt with, open the chest to find the pair of enchanted axes [Irkngthand War Axe of Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Irkngthand_War_Axe_of_Fire "Skyrim:Irkngthand War Axe of Fire") and [Irkngthand War Axe of Freezing](/wiki/Skyrim:Irkngthand_War_Axe_of_Freezing "Skyrim:Irkngthand War Axe of Freezing"), as well as other typical random chest treasure.

It will also unlock the ability to craft the [Irkngthand War Axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Irkngthand_War_Axe "Skyrim:Irkngthand War Axe"), a slightly superior brand of one-handed Dwarven War Axe, which appears to be basically as strong as a Glass War Axe but only requires the Dwarven Smithing perk. This is the base item of which you just received the two enchanted examples.

## Bugs

- The Dwemer spider ambush outside of Bronze Water Cave can be set off prematurely due to the spiders not actually being disabled prior to Beneath Bronze Waters. If set off prematurely, the quest will then be impossible to start because the spiders are required for the quest.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.9a, fixes this bug.
- The trigger box for Kinthal's Saints bandit camp at Bronze Water Cave may attempt to disable itself even though it's controlled by an enable parent.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.2, addresses this issue. The DisableWhenDone flag has been removed as it's also flagged DoOnce and won't trigger again anyway.

## Quest Stages

| Beneath Bronze Waters (ccBGSSSE001\_Misc\_Dwarven) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 0 |  | Calcelmo has heard fishermen's tales of a strange apparatus outside of Bronze Water Cave. He believes it is an ancient Dwemer mechanism of unknown purpose, waiting to be brought to life. I should investigate the area and see if there might be any way to trigger it. *Objective 0:* Investigate the entrance of Bronze Water Cave |
| 5 |  | I've arrived at the entrance of Bronze Water Cave. The fishermen that once fished here seem to have left behind a journal. It may contain a clue for activating the mechanisms nearby. *Objective 10:* Read the fisherman's journal |
| 10 |  | The fishermen at Bronze Water Cave saw faint glowing objects at the bottom of the lake near Bronze Water Cave, but they were unable to fish them up. They believed that a fishing rod of Dwarven make might be needed to retrieve them. They recently left for Alftand Ruined Tower, where the schematics for such a rod might be located. *Objective 15:* Find the Dwarven fishing rod schematic in Alftand Ruined Tower |
| 20 |  | I've found the schematics for the Dwarven fishing rod that might be used to catch the glowing objects that lie below the water's surface outside of Bronze Water Cave. I should return it to Calcelmo so that he can construct it. *Objective 18:* Bring the Dwarven fishing rod schematic to Calcelmo |
| 30 |  | I've given Calcelmo the schematics for the Dwarven fishing rod. I now need to wait for him to construct it. I should ask him about it at this time tomorrow. *Objective 20:* Wait 24 hours for Calcelmo to build the fishing rod |
| 40 |  | Calcelmo should be finished constructing the Dwarven fishing rod from the schematic I discovered. *Objective 25:* Return to Calcelmo |
| 90 |  | Calcelmo has given me the Dwarven fishing rod. I should cast it at the fishing spots near Bronze Water Cave so that I might be able to catch the objects that might activate the mechanisms near the cave. *Objective 30:* Use the dwarven fishing rod to catch the strange objects near Bronze Water Cave (0/2) |
| 100 |  | I cast the Dwarven fishing rod into the water near Bronze Water Cave, and caught an aetherium dynamo core. An empty socket on the pedestal nearby appears to be shaped to hold such a core. I'll have to insert the dynamo core to bring the rest of the mechanism to life. *Objective 50:* Insert the aetherium dynamo core into the dynamo actuator (0/2) |
| 300 | ☑ | After using the Dwarven fishing rod near Bronze Water Cave and powering up an ancient mechanism using aetherium dynamo cores, a pedestal rose from beneath the surface revealing a submerged chest. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 101, 200, 201, 400.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE001_Misc_Dwarven stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE001_Misc_Dwarven`.
