Birna's Oddments

**Birna's Oddments** is a general goods store in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold").

It is a two-story building, located between the [Jarl's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl%27s_Longhouse_(Winterhold) "Skyrim:Jarl's Longhouse (Winterhold)") and [Kraldar's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Kraldar%27s_House "Skyrim:Kraldar's House") and is home to [Birna](/wiki/Skyrim:Birna "Skyrim:Birna") and [Ranmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranmir "Skyrim:Ranmir"). It consists of only one zone, which is the [interior](#Birna.27s_Oddments) of the building.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Birna](/wiki/Skyrim:Birna "Skyrim:Birna") [General Goods](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "General Goods")  [Ranmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranmir "Skyrim:Ranmir") |

## Related Quests

- **[Yngol's Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol%27s_Barrow "Skyrim:Yngol's Barrow")**: Find the treasure unlocked by the [Coral Dragon Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Coral_Dragon_Claw "Skyrim:Coral Dragon Claw").

## Birna's Oddments

There is a row of pillars supporting a balcony at the front of the building and stairs up to it at the rear, to the right of a chicken coop containing a single [nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"). The main entrance leads directly into the shop, with the counter on your right, in front of the north wall. [Birna](/wiki/Skyrim:Birna "Skyrim:Birna") spends her day standing behind the counter. The first time you interact with her she will offer to sell you the [coral dragon claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Coral_Dragon_Claw "Skyrim:Coral Dragon Claw") for 50 septims. There are several barrels and sacks of [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") around the building, but no displayed merchandise in the shop. Once you have completed the relevant [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol%27s_Barrow "Skyrim:Yngol's Barrow"), or improved Birna's brother [Ranmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranmir "Skyrim:Ranmir")'s disposition, you will be able to take all low-value items freely from the shop and residence upstairs.

Opposite the entrance is a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front and a [mammoth tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Mammoth Tusk") on the mantelpiece. To the right of the fireplace is an unlocked display cabinet containing two each of [petty](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem"), [lesser](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem"), and [common](/wiki/Skyrim:Common_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Common Soul Gem") [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"). Above this are three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") hanging from a rack attached to the ceiling, two [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid"), two bunches of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear") and a bunch of [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam"). On the counter is a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), four loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), while under the counter is a copy of *[Dunmer of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmer_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Dunmer of Skyrim")*, another small coin purse, a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger").

Against the north wall is a cupboard holding two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), three bottles of wine, and eight bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). To the right is a set of shelves holding two [potions of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), a [potion of resist fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire"), two [flutes](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), six [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), and several cheese wheels. Against the east wall is a narrow wooden table with an [Orcish dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger") on top. To the left of the fireplace is a rack hanging from the ceiling holding four [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), with a set of shelves to the left of that, holding an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace") and a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"). Against the south wall is a flight of stairs up to the top floor, with a couple of crates and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") under the stairs.

Upstairs, against the west wall, is a long wooden table and bench, with three bottles of alto wine, two fillets of [salmon meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Meat "Skyrim:Salmon Meat"), a [chicken's egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), two bulbs of garlic, a couple of loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and several wedges of cheese on the table, and a loaf of bread on the bench. To the right is a small round wooden table and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing leveled items, with two more bottles of alto wine and five loose septims on top of the table. Coming out from the middle of the north wall is a large double bed with a dresser on either side, both containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), with a copy of the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Mystery of Talara, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystery_of_Talara,_v3 "Skyrim:Mystery of Talara, v3")* on top. At the foot of the bed is another chest also containing leveled items. Above the stairs, against the east wall, is a set of shelves, but they only hold clutter, with a door out onto the balcony to the left.

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in Birna's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. They are restocked every two days.

| Count | Item | Details |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ~3 | Leveled [Animal Parts](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Parts "Skyrim:Animal Parts") | Max 4 (4@75%) |
| ~0 | Leveled [Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems") | Max 1 (1@25%) |
| ~3 | Leveled [Enchanted Jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Apparel "Skyrim:Generic Magic Apparel") | Max 4 (4@75%) |
| ~0 | Leveled [Ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingots "Skyrim:Ingots") | Best-quality; Max 1 (1@25%) |
| ~1 | Leveled [Ores](/wiki/Skyrim:Ore "Skyrim:Ore")/[Charcoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Charcoal "Skyrim:Charcoal") | Max 1 (1@50%) |
| ~1 | Leveled [Potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") | Max 1 (1@50%) |
| ~1 | Leveled Soul Gems (empty and full) | Max 1 (1@75%) |
| ~6 | [Lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") | Max 8 (7@75% + 1@100%) |
| ~1 | Low-level [Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor") (unenchanted) | Max 1 (1@75%) |
| ~1 | Low-level [Weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") (unenchanted) | Max 1 (1@75%) |
| ~5 | [Torches](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch") | Best-quality; Max 10 (10@50%) |
| ~3 | [Miscellaneous Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Items "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Items") (clutter) | Max 4 (4@75%) |

## Notes

- Unlike other stores in the game, Birna's Oddments has no exterior sign.
- With the exception of some barrels and sacks, all containers in the area are [non-respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") and safe to store items in.
- The display case lid collides with the rabbits above it when opened (resulting in humorous motion on the part of the rabbits).

## Bugs

- The key to the store is named [Key to Ranmir's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Ranmir%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Ranmir's House") and is carried by both [Ranmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranmir "Skyrim:Ranmir") and [Birna](/wiki/Skyrim:Birna "Skyrim:Birna").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.0, addresses this issue. It renames it to "Key to Birna's Oddments".

# Skyrim:Birna

## Overview

| Birna (RefID: 0001C18C) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

Birna tending her shop

**Birna** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [pawnbroker](/wiki/Skyrim:Pawnbroker "Skyrim:Pawnbroker") who runs [Birna's Oddments](/wiki/Skyrim:Birna%27s_Oddments "Skyrim:Birna's Oddments") in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") and feels depressed about how little custom the shop has; her only regular customer is the [housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl"), [Thaena](/wiki/Skyrim:Thaena "Skyrim:Thaena"), who isn't the most friendly person. Her brother, [Ranmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranmir "Skyrim:Ranmir"), has a tendency to drink away their earnings.

Birna wears a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0001be1b "Skyrim:Boots"). She is equipped with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Ranmir%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Ranmir's House") to [Ranmir's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranmir%27s_House "Skyrim:Ranmir's House") as well as a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

Since Ranmir spends much of his time drinking inside the [Frozen Hearth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth"), Birna must dedicate most of her time to running the store in order to support both herself and her brother. She wakes up at 7am and unlocks the door to the store. She will then stand behind the counter in the store for the next thirteen hours, offering her services between 8:30am and 8pm. After a busy day of running the shop, she will leave at 8pm to head to the Frozen Hearth. She will find a seat and eat and drink with the other regulars for the next three hours. At 11pm, she will make her way back home. She will stay up for another hour, until heading upstairs to sleep for the next seven hours.

## Related Quests

- **[Yngol's Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol%27s_Barrow "Skyrim:Yngol's Barrow")**: Find the treasure unlocked by the [Coral Dragon Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Coral_Dragon_Claw "Skyrim:Coral Dragon Claw").

### Yngol's Barrow

If you ask her if she has ever had a bad deal after asking about her business, she will explain how she came to possess a seemingly useless [dragon claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Coral_Dragon_Claw "Skyrim:Coral Dragon Claw"):

:   **You said something about a bad deal?**
:   *"Yeah, it was stupid of me. I shouldn't have believed the story and just refused the trade. But I didn't, and now I'm stuck with this worthless junk."*
:   **What was the story?**
:   *"Some line about this claw thing and [Yngol Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol%27s_Barrow "Skyrim:Yngol's Barrow"). He said it was worth more than its weight in gold if I took it back there. Something about placing it back in Yngol's chamber, I don't know. What was I thinking? Even if it were true, I'm not setting foot in some ancient tomb, filled with who knows what."*
:   **I could look into it for you.**
:   *"I don't even care any more. You want to check it out? Fine. I'll sell you the thing for fifty gold, and then it's your problem."*
:   **I'll take that claw for 50 gold.**

If you try to buy it from her without enough money, she will say:

:   *"Oh, I'd gladly sell it to you if you had the money. But you don't, do you?"*

If you do have the required amount of gold, she will give you the dragon claw:

:   *"Fine, here you go. You get killed on account of this thing, it's not my fault. Got it? But, I suppose, if it does actually turn out to be worth something, let me know, will you?"*

Despite this request, you cannot inform her of the [true treasure](/wiki/Skyrim:Helm_of_Yngol "Skyrim:Helm of Yngol") the claw protects.

## Dialogue

Approaching Birna will have her inform you that almost everything she has is for sale and information about her brother:

:   *"I'll sell just about anything, if it's worth my time. Keep that in mind, will you?"*
:   *"I do what's necessary so we can get by. Have to, since I can't count on my brother for anything."*
:   *"If you're looking for Ranmir, he's either passed out in bed, or working on winding up that way."*
:   *"My brother's a good-for-nothing drunk. We'd have lost the house by now if it were up to him."*
:   *"Just because we live in the middle of nowhere doesn't give Ranmir the right to drink himself into oblivion."*
:   *"Ranmir has no problem drinking himself under the table, so I have to be the one to make ends meet."*

If you assist Ranmir in stopping himself from [drowning his sorrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Drowned_Sorrows "Skyrim:Drowned Sorrows"), she will instead make a series of comments about how her life has been improved now that her brother isn't drinking her profits away:

:   *"Things are easier now that I don't have to worry about Ranmir anymore."*
:   *"I still can't believe you were able to help Ranmir pull himself together."*
:   *"Without all our money going to drink, I can afford to expand my selection a bit."*

When speaking to Birna directly she can be asked questions:

:   **Why set up shop here?**
:   *"Wasn't by choice, I can tell you that. Options were in short supply. Ranmir and I grew up here, and nearly any money I make, he drinks away. Without the coin to pack up and leave, I decided to take to trading."*

:   **Do you get much business way up here?**
:   *"Very funny. I'm sure you've noticed that Winterhold isn't exactly overflowing with people. So I'll sell whatever I can. If it's worth putting a price on, you can bet I'll do it. I've been burned a few times, made a few bad deals, but mostly I come out on top."*

If you choose to invest in her business:

:   **I'd like to make an investment in your business.**
:   *"You want to give me money? Just like that? Fine, but I intend to earn that investment. I don't need handouts."*
:   **Let's see what you can do with this.**
:   *"I'll work hard to justify your faith in me."*

## Unused Dialogue

- Birna's dialogue after the end of [Drowned Sorrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Drowned_Sorrows "Skyrim:Drowned Sorrows") doesn't change to mention that [Ranmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranmir "Skyrim:Ranmir") is gone. She was supposed to expand upon her previous response if asked about why she set up shop in Winterhold after the quest was completed, but there was nothing put in the scripting to allow the updated line to be said:

:   *"Wasn't by choice, I can tell you that. Options were in short supply. Ranmir and I grew up here, and his drinking soaked up whatever coin we had. So I opened a shop to try and get by. Now, though... Have to admit, I'm attached to the place. Suppose that makes me crazy, doesn't it?"*

    -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.

## Conversations

Birna and Ranmir, arguing

The first time you enter into Winterhold, you may encounter Birna and Ranmir arguing on the road:

:   **Birna**: *"We need coin, Ranmir, and you're not bringing home any."*
:   **Ranmir**: *"And you'd have me do what, join the [College](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") and prance about casting spells all day?"*
:   **Birna**: *"Don't just walk away from me! Where do you think you're going?"*
:   **Ranmir**: *"To the [Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth") for a drink, of course! Where else could I even go in this gods-forsaken town?"*
:   **Birna**: *"And what, you think that'll solve all your problems?"*
:   **Ranmir**: *"Probably not, but it's worth a try!"*

Birna and Thaena having a discussion

Birna will have a few different conversations with [Thaena](/wiki/Skyrim:Thaena "Skyrim:Thaena"), during her visits:

:   **Birna**: *"How are you today, Thaena?"*
:   **Thaena**: *"Same as ever. Trying to keep from freezing to death, trying to keep food on the table."*
:   **Birna**: *"Always looking on the bright side, aren't you."*
:   **Thaena**: *"Don't sass me, little girl."*

:   **Thaena**: *"You got anything in here worth buying?"*
:   **Birna**: *"I certainly hope so, otherwise I'm wasting my time."*
:   **Thaena**: *"Yeah, well I don't see anything."*

Birna and Enthir, talking business

She can also converse with [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir") about business between the two:

:   **Birna**: *"You looking for anything in particular this time?"*
:   **Enthir**: *"Perhaps, perhaps. I'm not quite sure what I need."*
:   **Birna**: *"Well, you know the drill. You don't see it here, it's gonna cost you extra for me to get it."*
:   **Enthir**: *"I'm fully aware of the terms of our... arrangement."*

:   **Enthir**: *"Have you gotten the items I requested from you?"*
:   **Birna**: *"Not yet. You know you're asking for some pretty strange stuff, don't you? It's not easy to find."*
:   **Enthir**: *"You assured me that you could find it, however."*
:   **Birna**: *"I did, and I will. It's just tougher than I thought."*

Should she meet with Ranmir inside The Frozen Hearth, she will either angrily ask about their money or desperately try to get him to return home:

:   **Birna**: *"Well, isn't this a surprise!"*
:   **Birna**: *"How much of our money have you spent today, Ranmir? Anything left, or is it all gone?"*
:   **Ranmir**: *"If I wanted to get yelled at, I'd be home. Can't you leave me be?"*
:   **Birna**: *"Oh, I'm sorry. Am I bothering you? Am I making your life more difficult?"*

:   **Birna**: *"Please, come home. Just... Just come home."*
:   **Ranmir**: *"Can't. Got at least two rounds to go."*
:   **Ranmir**: *"Why don't you go... sell something."*
:   **Birna**: *"Why? Because I'd rather be here trying to keep my only brother from drinking himself to death."*
:   **Ranmir**: *"Ha! Drink ain't gonna kill me. Not today, anyway."*

[Haran](/wiki/Skyrim:Haran "Skyrim:Haran") will also mention the conflicts between Ranmir and Birna in a conversation with [Dagur](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagur "Skyrim:Dagur"):

:   **Haran**: *"How long are we going to let Ranmir drink himself into a stupor? When will enough be enough?"*
:   **Dagur**: *"As long as he keeps paying, I suppose. He keeps to himself, and isn't hurting anyone."*
:   **Haran**: *"Are you so sure of that? I think Birna might disagree with you."*
:   **Dagur**: *"It's not my place to get involved in their family's business, remember? You're the one that told me to stay out of it."*

## Rumors

Dagur will suggest you visit her shop if you ask him for information about Winterhold:

:   *"I'm afraid there's not much to be said. Winterhold is hardly what it used to be. You can talk to Birna if you need to buy anything. She doesn't have much, but could certainly use the coin. And then there's our little inn. Most of the business we get is from folks here to visit the [College](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"), though even that's dried up some."*

## Notes

- Birna *technically* isn't related to the quest Yngol's Barrow at all. All of her dialogue is stored in a different quest, [A Bad Trade](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Bad_Trade "Skyrim:A Bad Trade"), internally known as `FreeformWinterholdA`, and is internally defined as belonging to this quest as well. However, the quest ultimately goes unused in the final game, despite the fact that purchasing the coral claw advances the quest to stage 20. No other scripts update it. The dev notes attached to the quest stages list the purchased item as "the jar" but are otherwise in-line with the events that transpire in the final game. This "jar" would've actually been a [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Unobtainable_Items#Other_Unobtainable_Items "Skyrim:Unobtainable Items") which still exists in the files, and gets checked for by a trigger associated with the quest.
  - A dev note attached to stage 10 of Yngol's Barrow still references the freeform quest, reading: *"if the player enters Yngol barrow before getting the related FF quest in Winterhold, just never have that appear."*
- If you talk to Birna enough times in rapid succession, she may say phrases said by Winterhold Guards.

## Bugs

- Birna may just stay outside with Ranmir while in Winterhold, negating the option of trading with her. See [the discussion page](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Birna "Skyrim talk:Birna") for details on possible workarounds.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.0, addresses this issue. The navmesh inside the shop was bad, preventing her from using the door.
- If you buy the Coral Dragon Claw off Birna and then speak to her again when you have less than 50 gold, Birna will have dialogue offering to sell the claw again as if she still had it.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.6, fixes this bug.

Bits and Pieces

**Bits and Pieces** is the general goods store in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") run by [Sayma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sayma "Skyrim:Sayma").

It is next door to [Radiant Raiment](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant_Raiment "Skyrim:Radiant Raiment"), on the corner by the market square. It contains only one zone, the [interior](#Bits_and_Pieces).

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Kayd](/wiki/Skyrim:Kayd "Skyrim:Kayd")  [Sayma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sayma "Skyrim:Sayma") [General Goods](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "General Goods") |

## Bits and Pieces

The entrance leads directly into the shop, with a wooden bench and small round table on the left. The counter is at the far end of the room in front of the south wall. All of the items on display around the shop are [Displayed Merchandise](#Displayed_Merchandise), with the exception of any items in [containers](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers "Skyrim:Containers") or in the display cabinets, the herbs hanging from the ceiling, a loose [septim](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") under the counter, and another loose septim on the shelves behind the counter. The herbs hanging from the ceiling are a total of seven [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, and three bunches of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"). Against the west wall is an expert-locked display cabinet containing a [Dwarven dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"), a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") and a leveled [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Warhammer "Skyrim:Warhammer"). There is a second expert-locked display cabinet containing a leveled [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword") (up to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric")) (see [bugs](#Bugs)) and a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"). There is a chair between these two cabinets, where you will often find [Sayma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sayma "Skyrim:Sayma") sitting upon entering the store. There is a central pillar supporting the vaunted ceiling and in the northwestern corner is a cooking fire at eye level with an empty metal pot in front of it and two more hanging above it inside, with a set of double doors leading to the residence.

Through the doors into the residence there is a wooden bench under two wall shelves on the left, on the south wall, with a couple of pieces of cheese on them and a common book on the bench. In the northeastern corner is a cupboard holding two [sweet rolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), a bowl containing [tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"), a haunch of raw [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison"), three loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and several pieces of cheese, with a wall shelf on the east wall to the right of it holding crockery. To the left of the cupboard, against the north wall, is a bookcase holding six common books, a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute") and a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), while in the northwestern corner is a long wooden table and two chairs, with a potion of regeneration, a bunch of tundra cotton, a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), a loaf of bread, a couple of wheels of cheese and two loose septims on top. To the left of this, along the west wall, is a wooden bench with a small unit holding a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") separating the table and bench. To the south is a stairwell with a flight up to the top floor and a flight down to the cellar.

Halfway up there is a large vase with a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush planted in it. At the top of the stairs is a L-shaped balcony with two doors off of it on the west wall. In front of you is a small seating area with a low chair, square wooden table and small round table in the corner with an iron dagger on top. On the square table is a plate of bread and cheese with a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and a [goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"). Around the corner is a narrow table with a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") of bread and a plate with two tomatoes and an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge") on top. Above this is a wall shelf holding a bunch of elves ear. At the northern end of the balcony is a bookcase holding eleven common books, a potion of health and a flute, with a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") beside it and a chair in front.

The first door opens into a bedroom containing a single bed in the northwestern corner with an open crate at the foot of it containing a bunch of tundra cotton. There is also a small round table with the [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger") on top. To the right against the east wall is a small wardrobe with a set of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") on top and a washbasin on a stand beside it. In the southwestern corner is a tall wardrobe containing fine clothes, with a wall shelf, chair and small wardrobe along the south wall, while opposite the small wardrobe is a small cupboard with an apprentice-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") containing random items on top of it.

The second door leads to another bedroom with a single bed in the southeastern corner, and small square table beside it with three loose septims on top. At the foot of the bed is another open crate containing a bunch of tundra cotton. To the right of the bed, against the south wall is a set of shelves holding three [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"), a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), with a potion of regeneration on top and a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots") beside it. Against the north wall is a small wardrobe, with a tall one against the west wall to the left. Opposite the door is a small cupboard containing clutter and with a narrow table to the left, behind the door. On this is an iron dagger and a bowl containing a bunch of tundra cotton and above is a wall shelf holding a set of clothes.

Descending to the cellar leads to a storage area with food barrels, an archery target with a square wooden table with a set of [banded iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Banded Iron Armor") and a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield") on top in the northwestern corner, while in the southeastern corner is a square wooden table with a [goat hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Hide "Skyrim:Goat Hide") (see [bugs](#Bugs)) on it and a cupboard with a couple of loaves of bread, several pieces of cheese and a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg") on the shelves and an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword") on top. To the left along the east wall is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing leveled items.

## Displayed Merchandise

The following items are sitting out in the store, for example on the store counters. They can be purchased from the merchant, or else can be stolen. Other items may also be present in the store, but those other items are not available for purchase. They [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") after ten days.

|  |
| --- |
| - **Apparel**: 1 [Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"), 1 [Fine Clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"), - **Potions**: 1 [Draught of Strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Strength "Skyrim:Draught of Strength"), 1 [Potion of Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"), 1 [Potion of Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), 1 [Potion of Minor Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), 1 [Potion of Plentiful Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Healing"), 1 [Potion of Regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), - **Food**: 2 [Gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), 2 [Leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), 5 [Tomato](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato") - **Ingredients**: 1 [Blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), 2 [Canis Root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), 4 [Deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell"), 1 [Dragon's Tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue"), 1 [Fly Amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), 4 [Garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), 2 [Lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), 2 [Rock Warbler Egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), 1 [Thistle Branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch"), 1 [Tundra Cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") - **Books**: 1 *[Beggar Prince](/wiki/Lore:Beggar_Prince "Lore:Beggar Prince")*, 1 *[Biography of Barenziah v1, v2, v3](/wiki/Lore:Biography_of_Barenziah "Lore:Biography of Barenziah")*, 1 *[Nightingales: Fact or Fiction?](/wiki/Lore:Nightingales:_Fact_or_Fiction%3F "Lore:Nightingales: Fact or Fiction?")* - **Misc**: 2 [Basket](/wiki/Skyrim:Basket "Skyrim:Basket"), 2 [Bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl"), 1 [Cave Bear Pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Cave_Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Cave Bear Pelt"), 1 [Clothes Iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes_Iron "Skyrim:Clothes Iron"), 2 [Cup](/wiki/Skyrim:Cup "Skyrim:Cup"), 1 [Drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"), 1 [Horker Tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk"), 1 [Jug](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug"), 1 [Skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Skull "Skyrim:Skull"), 1 [Snow Bear Pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Snow Bear Pelt"), 1 [Tankard](/wiki/Skyrim:Tankard "Skyrim:Tankard") |

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in Bits and Pieces' [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every two days.

| Count | Item | Details |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ~4 | Leveled [Animal Parts](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Parts "Skyrim:Animal Parts") | Max 5 (5@75%) |
| ~1 | Leveled [Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems") | Max 2 (2@25%) |
| ~3 | Leveled [Enchanted Jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Apparel "Skyrim:Generic Magic Apparel") | Max 4 (4@75%) |
| ~1 | Leveled [Ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingots "Skyrim:Ingots") | Max 5 (5@25%) |
| ~1 | Leveled Jewelry (unenchanted) or [Amulet of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Amulets_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Specialty Gear") | Max 2 (2@25%) |
| ~3 | Leveled [Ores](/wiki/Skyrim:Ore "Skyrim:Ore")/[Charcoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Charcoal "Skyrim:Charcoal") | Max 5 (5@50%) |
| ~11 | Leveled [Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") (empty and full) | Max 15 (15@75%) |
| ~6 | [Lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") | Max 8 (7@75% + 1@100%) |
| ~11 | Low-level [Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor") (unenchanted) | Max 15 (15@75%) |
| ~15 | Low-level [Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows") (batches of 10) | Max 20 (20@75%) |
| ~5 | Low-level [Weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") (unenchanted) | Max 7 (7@75%) |
| ~4 | [Miscellaneous Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Items "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Items") (clutter) | Max 5 (5@75%) |
| 1 | [Potion of Cure Disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Potion of Cure Disease") |  |
| ~8 | [Potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") | Max 15 (15@50%) |
| ~3 | Random Novice [Spell Tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes") | Max 5 (5@50%) |
| ~5 | [Torches](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch") | Max 10 (10@50%) |

## Notes

- There is a  "Loot") Loot [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the bottom left of the entrance door.
- Aside from some barrels and sacks, all containers in the area are [non-respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") and safe to store items in.
- This building appears in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online") as [Bountiful Goods](/wiki/Online:Bountiful_Goods "Online:Bountiful Goods").
- If you arrive for the first time at Solitude during the day (open store hours), Bits and Pieces will be the only store (aside from the inn) that will be open, as the others will be closed so the owners or employees can witness Roggvir's execution.

## Bugs

- The greatsword may be laying on top of the glass instead of inside. **?**
- You can't interact with the goat hide in the cellar.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.

Bjartur, in the Castle Dour Dungeon

**Bjartur** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [prisoner](/wiki/Skyrim:Prisoner_(class) "Skyrim:Prisoner (class)") found in [Castle Dour Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour_Dungeon "Skyrim:Castle Dour Dungeon") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), apparently jailed for being a staunch supporter of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks").

She wears a [roughspun tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Roughspun_Tunic "Skyrim:Roughspun Tunic") and carries a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic").

Without anything to do inside her jail cell, her daily routine involves standing in one place, at times conversing with the patrolling jailor and headsman [Ahtar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahtar "Skyrim:Ahtar") through the bars. She sleeps from midnight to 8am.

## Dialogue

While you are in the dungeon during her waking hours, you were meant to hear her loudly exclaim the following lines, which can't play due to a [bug](#Bugs):

:   *"You won't get anything out of me, you filthy sons o' horkers."*
:   *"I stand with the Stormcloaks. You Imperial dogs will never break my will. Never!"*

If you attempt to talk to her through the bars she will defiantly say:

:   *"You here for my next interrogation? I got nothing but time..."*
:   *"Leave me be, Imperial. I haven't got anything to say to you."*
:   *"Don't think I don't know what's coming."*
:   *"It's only a matter of time before Ahtar's blade finds my neck..."*

## Unused Dialogue

Because it is impossible to engage in conversation with her, these two farewells will never be heard:

:   *"Tell these Horkers to set me free."*
:   *"Leave me be. I'm no harm here."*

## Unused Scenes

- During his daily routine, headsman Ahtar was supposed to engage in conversation with Bjartur. However, the two conversations will never be heard due to several developer oversights:
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.

:   **Ahtar**: *"Rest up, scum. Probably getting executed tomorrow."*
:   **Bjartur**: *"Yeah, you said that yesterday."*
:   **Ahtar**: *"Come now. You'll want to show up in Sovngarde refreshed. You got an eternity of merrimakin' ahead of you."* **or**
     *"Guess the headsman's been busy with all your friends. Ha ha ha ha ha!"*

:   **Bjartur**: *"Hey, jailor! What I don't understand is why you're siding with the Imperials."*
:   **Ahtar**: *"Shut up, scum."*
:   **Bjartur**: *"I mean, the Redguards fought off the Aldmeri and the Empire, and now Hammerfell is an independent state. That's all we Nords want for Skyrim!"*
:   **Ahtar**: *"I said shut up, scum!"*
:   **Bjartur**: *"So it's okay if your people rebel against the Empire, but not mine?"*
:   **Ahtar**: *"They aren't my "people." I'm with the Empire because they pay me. And that means I'm out here, and you're in there. So shut up, scum!"*

## Bugs

- Her two idle yelling lines have a condition attached that they only play while on the package `SolitudeBlacksmithWorkDay8x14`. However, seeing as Bjartur doesn't use said package at any point (as she doesn't work at the [Solitude Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Blacksmith "Skyrim:Solitude Blacksmith") and has no ties to it at all), they go unused.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.

## Notes

- Bjartur will never get released, not even if the Stormcloaks take over Solitude.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, addresses this issue. She is disabled from the game in case of a Stormcloak victory.
- For some reason, she is one of only a handful of people that have a relationship set up with [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke"). They are marked as rivals.
